# cs.DB [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Accelerating Point-in-Polygon Predicates via Algebraic Hash-Joins and Discrete Global Grids at Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08956)
*Levente Juhasz*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 本文探讨了基于离散全球网格系统（DGGS）替代传统向量点面包含查询的方法，并通过交互式仪表盘在DuckDB上对四种DGGS实现（H3、S2、A5、ISEA4H）进行性能评估，证明预索引数据可消除编码开销，使所有DGGS实现均能达到亚秒级连接延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于向量的点面包含查询依赖计算昂贵的几何谓词，即使使用空间索引，在面对大规模数据集时扩展性依然较差。DGGS提供了可扩展的替代方案，但当前网格实现存在显著的性能"工具差距"。

Method: 构建交互式仪表盘，在DuckDB上对四种DGGS实现（H3、S2、A5、ISEA4H）进行渐进式场景评估，可视化即时编码的开销，并展示预索引如何消除这一开销。

Result: 当数据经过预索引后，无论DGGS的数学复杂度或工具成熟度如何，所有实现都能达到亚秒级连接延迟，充分发挥现代向量化执行引擎的吞吐能力。

Conclusion: 预索引是消除DGGS编码开销、实现高性能空间查询的关键；DGGS结合现代向量化执行引擎可作为传统几何谓词查询的可扩展替代方案。

Abstract: Traditional vector-based point-in-polygon queries rely on computationally expensive geometric predicates that scale poorly for massive datasets, even when accelerated by spatial indices. Discrete Global Grid Systems (DGGS) offer a scalable alternative by discretizing geometries into hierarchical cells, transforming complex spatial relations into constant-time relational hash-joins. However, adopting a DGGS introduces an overhead to encode data, and current grid implementations exhibit a significant performance ``tooling gap.'' In this demonstration, we present an interactive dashboard that empirically evaluates these computational tradeoffs across four DGGS implementations (H3, S2, A5, and ISEA4H) using DuckDB. Through progressive scenarios, the platform visualizes the overhead of on-the-fly encoding and demonstrates how pre-indexing spatial datasets eliminates this overhead. Ultimately, the demo proves that when data is pre-indexed, all DGGS regardless of their mathematical complexity or tooling converge to sub-second join latencies, unlocking the throughput of modern vectorized execution engines.

</details>


### [2] [Taxonomy Maintenance In The Wild Over Evolving Scholarly Data: Reliability, Efficiency, and Cost-Effectiveness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09149)
*Daomin Ji,Hui Luo,Zhifeng Bao,Junhao Gan,Zi Huang*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出GIST框架，利用论文"相关工作"章节提取局部层次结构，在几何盒嵌入空间中整合为全局分类体系，实现学术分类法的持续动态维护，在arXiv数据集上以极低成本和运行时间显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有学术分类法构建方法多为静态，无法适应快速增长的科研论文流，需要一种能在持续演化中维护分类体系的方案。

Method: 从论文"相关工作"章节提取局部层次结构，在盒嵌入空间中融合为全局分类体系；学习词嵌入与盒嵌入的双向映射；采用新颖性感知的核心集选择实现增量更新；结合假设概念生成器和低成本证据检索模块处理高速论文流。

Result: 在真实arXiv数据集上，GIST的Node F1和Edge F1分别比最强基线提升11.0%和13.1%，运行时间仅需基线的9.6%，成本仅需12.7%。

Conclusion: 通过将结构归纳锚定于专家策展的证据（相关工作章节），结合几何嵌入空间和高效增量机制，GIST在低成本下实现了卓越的分类法维护性能。

Abstract: The rapid growth of scientific publications makes scholarly taxonomies quickly obsolete. We study taxonomy maintenance in the wild, a new problem that moves beyond static construction by continuously adapting taxonomies to evolving scholarly repositories, such as arXiv, for a given research topic. We propose GIST, a robust framework for maintaining evolving taxonomies. Unlike purely LLM-centric approaches, GIST grounds structure induction in expert-curated evidence by extracting partial hierarchies from the "Related Work" sections of papers. It integrates these partial taxonomies into a unified global taxonomy in a geometric box-embedding space, where box containment encodes the inductive bias of is-a relations. To connect semantics with geometric structure, GIST learns a bidirectional mapping between word embeddings and box embeddings. For efficient incremental updates, GIST uses novelty-aware coreset selection to update the model with representative historical signals and new evidence, avoiding costly full retraining. To handle high-velocity paper streams under user-specific token budgets, GIST further combines a hypothesized concept generator with a cost-effective evidence retrieval module. Experiments on real-world arXiv datasets show that GIST outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, improving Node F1 and Edge F1 by 11.0% and 13.1% over the strongest baseline while requiring only 9.6% of its runtime and 12.7% of its monetary cost.

</details>


### [3] [SQL-RewriteBench: A Correctness-Gated, Full-Denominator Benchmark for Statement-Level SQL Rewriting [Experiment,Analysis & Benchmark]](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09251)
*Jiang Long,Tianci Gao,Shiyuan Hao,Haochen Zhang,Shuncheng Liu,Jiang Zhang*

Main category: cs.DB

TL;DR: 提出了SQL-RewriteBench，这是一个专门评估SQL重写方法能否真正部署的基准，包含180个实例和全面指标，结果发现现有方法在实际部署场景中表现不佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SQL重写基准要么聚焦DBMS性能、规则回归、查询等价或方言翻译，缺少从接收输入查询到生成可执行、结果一致且实际可用的重写这一完整路径的评估。研究者希望弥补这一缺口，提供面向部署的重写评估框架。

Method: 设计了SQL-RewriteBench基准，包含180个可执行基准实例（EQUIV/PERF/ROBUST/DIALECT四个池），提出了SCS（静态SQL结构确定性索引）和CGOQ（正确性门控优化质量分数）两个核心指标，采用正确性门控和全分母记账方法，明确分离源接受率、生成率、执行覆盖率、结果一致性、不安全重写率和加速分布六个维度。

Result: 在七个代表方法（学术和基于LLM的）上测试，所有方法的全基准CGOQ均为负值。现有方法常常在重写前就失败、未通过结果检查，或者返回正确的重写但比原始查询更慢或没有提升。

Conclusion: 可部署的SQL重写需要更广泛的输入处理能力、结果验证机制以及能意识到收益的重写决策，当前方法在这些方面均存在明显不足。

Abstract: Statement-level SQL rewriting can improve query performance and maintainability without changing the DBMS kernel, but existing benchmarks do not evaluate rewrite methods as deployable systems. They typically focus on DBMS performance, rule regression, query equivalence, or dialect translation, while missing the full path from accepting an input query to producing an executable, result-consistent, and operationally useful rewrite. We present SQL-RewriteBench, a benchmark for statement-level SQL rewriting that applies correctness gating and full-denominator accounting. Its metric suite explicitly separates Source Acceptance, Generation Rate, Execution Coverage, Result Consistency, UnsafeRewrite Rate, and speedup distribution. It also defines SCS, a deterministic index of static SQL structure, and CGOQ, a correctness-gated optimization-quality score that gives optimization credit only after the case-specific Checker Contract is satisfied. CGOQ combines runtime improvement with structural simplification through a continuous scoring function, making it suitable for deployment-oriented rewrite assessment. As an artifact, SQL-RewriteBench provides 180 executable Benchmark Instances organized into EQUIV, PERF, ROBUST, and DIALECT pools, each packaged with SQL, schema metadata, provenance, evidence, and rewrite-opportunity documentation. Across seven representative academic and LLM-based methods, every full-benchmark CGOQ is negative. Existing methods often fail before rewriting, fail result checks, or return correct rewrites that are slower or no better than the input. These results show that deployable SQL rewrite requires broader input handling, result validation, and benefit-aware rewrite decisions.

</details>

# cs.DC [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [SiFAR: Synchronization-Free All-Reduce for Low-Latency LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08973)
*Hritvik Taneja,Anish Saxena,Abhishek Revinipati,Jae Hyung Ju,Neal C. Crago,Moinuddin Qureshi*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出 SiFAR（无同步全规约），通过消除全规约中的同步障碍来降低低延迟推理中的通信开销。核心创新包括：双缓冲消除底部障碍、冗余拉取提升扩展性、投机规约减少顶部障碍。在 Llama-3.1-8B 上全规约延迟降低 52%，端到端吞吐提升 18.6%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理模型和智能体系统的兴起使 LLM 的 token 生成延迟成为关键瓶颈。与聊天机器人不同，这类系统生成的中间推理 token 不被人类消费，因此每个 token 的延迟直接决定端到端响应时间。低延迟推理使用最小批处理，使 token 生成受带宽约束。张量并行通过将模型权重分片到多个 GPU 来解决，但扩展到更多 GPU 时，All-Reduce 开销随 GPU 数量增长。

Method: 1）双缓冲：通过协同设计通信与模型执行，消除 oneshot 算法中的底部 WAW 依赖屏障；2）冗余拉取：利用现代交换机的 in-switch reduction 能力，每个 GPU 在交换机处完成完整规约，提升 oneshot 扩展性；3）投机规约：利用多轮 All-Reduce 操作间 GPU 紧密同步的特性，在顶部屏障前发起数据传输，通过轻量验证保证正确性。

Result: SiFAR 将 All-Reduce 延迟降低最高 52%，端到端吞吐提升：Llama-3.1-8B 提升 18.6%，Qwen3.5-397B-17B 提升 13.1%（TP=8）。

Conclusion: 通过消除同步障碍，SiFAR 有效降低了张量并行中的通信开销，为低延迟推理场景提供了高效的全规约方案，尤其适用于推理模型和智能体系统。

Abstract: The rise of reasoning models and agentic systems has made LLM token-generation latency a key bottleneck. Unlike chatbots, whose latency gains saturate at human reading speed, these systems generate intermediate reasoning tokens not consumed by humans. Thus, per-token latency directly determines end-to-end response time. Low-latency inference uses minimal batching, making token generation bandwidth-bound. Tensor Parallelism addresses this by sharding model weights across GPUs and loading them in parallel. However, scaling to more GPUs introduces All-Reduce overheads that grow with GPU count. Removing All-Reduce improves token throughput by 43% for Llama-3.1-8B on 8 H200 GPUs.
  We propose Synchronization-Free All-Reduce (SiFAR), which reduces synchronization overhead during low-latency inference. Existing oneshot and twoshot algorithms incur overheads from barriers before and after communication. First, we find that the bottom barrier in oneshot enforces a WAW dependency and eliminate it by co-designing communication and model execution to enable dual buffering. However, oneshot scales poorly with GPU count. Twoshot performs better at higher TP degrees but incurs an unavoidable bottom barrier. To overcome this, we leverage in-switch reduction in modern switches. We propose redundant pull, where each GPU reduces the full All-Reduce payload at the switch. This improves oneshot scalability while retaining its no-bottom-barrier advantage. Finally, to reduce top-barrier overhead, we observe that each decode step issues multiple All-Reduce operations, keeping GPUs tightly synchronized after the first. We therefore propose speculative reduction, which initiates data transfer before the top barrier and ensures correctness via lightweight validation. SiFAR reduces All-Reduce latency by up to 52% and improves end-to-end throughput by 18.6% for Llama-3.1-8B and 13.1% for Qwen3.5-397B-17B at TP=8.

</details>


### [5] [Distributed Symmetry Breaking on Hyperbolic Random Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09170)
*Yannic Maus,Janosch Ruff,Sonia Simons,George Skretas*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究双曲随机图（HRG）上的分布式算法。虽然Δ+1着色问题只需2轮即可解决，但本文证明最大独立集（MIS）和最大匹配（MM）问题在HRG上存在Ω(log log n / log log log n)的下界，并设计了上界为Õ(log^{5/3} log n)的算法，证明下界是多项式紧的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 观察到许多算法在真实网络上表现优于最坏情况保证，作者希望在更符合真实网络特性的双曲随机图模型下，系统研究分布式算法的性能边界。

Method: （1）通过证明HRG包含高度和度数较大的d-ary树结构，将已有的不可能性结果迁移到HRG上，得到下界；（2）设计针对HRG结构的MIS和MM分布式算法，达到Õ(log^{5/3} log n)轮。

Result: MIS和MM在HRG上的下界为Ω(log log n / log log log n)；上界为Õ(log^{5/3} log n)，优于一般图上的最坏情况界Ω(min{log Δ, √log n})。

Conclusion: 即使在结构良好的HRG模型上，MIS和MM本质上比Δ+1着色更困难；但HRG的特殊结构仍允许比一般图更高效的算法。

Abstract: Real-world networks like the internet share patterns like a power law degree distribution and a high clustering coefficient. Many of these properties are captured by the generative model of hyperbolic random graphs (HRGs), which provides a theoretical framework for studying such networks. Motivated by the observation that several algorithms perform better on real-world networks than their worst-case guarantees suggest, we design and analyse distributed algorithms under the assumption that the input graph is an HRG. Indeed, prior work has shown that the classical symmetry-breaking problem of $Δ+1$ colouring, where $Δ$ is the maximum degree of the graph, can be solved in 2 rounds on HRGs [Maus and Ruff; SODA'26].
  In stark contrast to this 2-round algorithm for $Δ+1$ colouring, we prove that the related symmetry-breaking problems of maximal independent set (MIS) and maximal matching (MM) are substantially harder: we establish a lower bound of $Ω\left(\frac{\log\log n}{\log\log\log n}\right)$ for MIS and MM on HRGs. Our lower bound techniques rely on new structural insights that may be of independent interest: we show that HRGs contain $d$-ary trees with large height and degree which enables us to adapt and lift prior impossibility results for distributed algorithms to the setting of HRGs.
  We also show that these lower bounds are polynomial tight: we design algorithms tailored to HRGs that solve MIS and MM in $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(\log^{5/3}\log n)$ rounds with high probability in the LOCAL model, improving over the general worst-case lower bound of $Ω\left(\min\left\{\log Δ, \sqrt{\log n}\right\}\right)$ rounds [Khoury and Schild; FOCS'25].

</details>


### [6] [Bidirectional Resource Scheduling for Disaggregated and Asynchronous RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09207)
*Tan Zhiqiang,Wang Maoxin,Wang Sijie,Yin Yiming,Wang Qiang,Chu Xiaowen,Shi Shaohuai*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出BiDiRL，一种面向异步、解耦RL的混合时空复用架构，通过热切换运行时、调度感知规划器和双向调度器，在不影响收敛性的情况下，将RL训练吞吐量提升最高1.94倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有高性能RL框架（如StreamRL、AReaL）采用解耦架构和异步rollout，但在不同硬件配置、模型规模、延迟水平和超参数下，rollout和训练资源仍经常出现空闲期，资源利用率不足。

Method: 1) 热切换运行时：实现rollout与训练资源间低开销的快速切换；2) 静态调度感知规划器：基于时间-性能模型选择利于热切换的资源划分，粗粒度平衡rollout与训练时长；3) 双向调度器：运行时通过细粒度资源切换，让瓶颈阶段临时借用另一资源池的空闲资源。

Result: 在两种32-GPU测试平台上，面对多种工作负载、数据集和模型，BiDiRL相比veRL、AReaL、ROLL等RL系统，训练吞吐量提升最高1.94倍，且不影响收敛行为。

Conclusion: BiDiRL通过混合时空复用有效地减少了异步解耦RL中rollout和训练双端资源的空闲时间，显著提升了吞吐量，是一种实用的RL训练加速架构。

Abstract: It is well established that the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs) can be improved by applying reinforcement learning (RL) in a post-training stage. In a standard RL iteration, the current model (the policy) generates experience through rollouts, and the resulting data is then used to update the policy during training. High-performance RL frameworks such as StreamRL and AReaL employ a disaggregated architecture and asynchronous rollouts to better exploit both rollout and training resources, thereby increasing overall system throughput.
  Nonetheless, across varying RL setups (e.g., hardware configurations, model scales, staleness levels, and hyperparameters) and under changing workloads, it remains common for both rollout and training resources to experience idle periods.
  In this paper, we present BiDiRL, a hybrid time-space multiplexing architecture for asynchronous, disaggregated RL designed to reduce resource idleness. First, we develop a hot-switch runtime that enables rapid switching between rollout and training resources with negligible overhead. Second, we propose a static, scheduling-aware planner based on time-performance modeling that chooses a hot-switch-friendly resource partition, so that rollout and training durations are roughly balanced at a coarse level. Third, at execution time, we introduce a bidirectional scheduler that further exploits runtime bubbles through fine-grained resource switching, allowing the bottleneck stage to temporarily borrow idle resources from the other pool. Across a wide range of workloads, datasets, and models on two 32-GPU testbeds, BiDiRL increases RL training throughput by up to 1.94x compared with RL systems including veRL, AReaL, and ROLL, without affecting convergence behavior.

</details>


### [7] [EcoKube: Simulating Carbon-Aware Scheduling Policies in Heterogeneous Edge-Cloud Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09318)
*Gonçalo Ferreira,Shashikant Ilager*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: EcoKube是一个用于评估异构边缘-云环境中可持续性调度策略的可配置仿真框架，支持事件驱动模拟、策略钩子和异构感知参考策略，并通过合成批处理工作负载评估了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有碳感知调度方案缺乏一致的、可复现的工作流来评估异构联邦边缘-云拓扑下的可持续性调度策略，导致不同策略之间难以进行公平比较。

Method: 提出EcoKube框架，包含事件驱动确定性模拟器、策略钩子（policy hooks）和异构感知参考策略。支持在混合边缘-云环境中考虑时间/地点变动的电网碳强度（CI）、站点PUE和异构硬件特性。

Result: 通过合成批处理工作负载，将参考策略与默认Kubernetes调度器、KEIDS和TOPSIS/KCSS进行了对比评估。

Conclusion: EcoKube提供了一种可复现的方式来在部署前比较可持续性感知调度策略，具有架构和实验两方面的贡献。

Abstract: Energy demand from cloud and edge computing is rising rapidly, with AI workloads further intensifying electricity use and associated carbon emissions. In hybrid edge-cloud settings, sustainability impact depends on time- and location-varying grid Carbon Intensity (CI), site Power Usage Effectiveness (PUE), and heterogeneous hardware characteristics. Existing carbon-aware work explores solutions such as temporal elasticity, spatio-temporal workload shifting, and carbon-aware placement across distributed sites. However, these solutions do not provide a consistent and reproducible workflow for evaluating sustainability-aware scheduling policies on heterogeneous, federated edge-cloud topologies. We present EcoKube: a configurable simulation framework for the reproducible evaluation of sustainability-aware scheduling policies in heterogeneous edge-cloud environments. The framework includes an event-driven deterministic simulator, policy hooks, and a heterogeneity-aware reference policy. We evaluate the framework with synthetic batch workloads, comparing the reference policy against the default Kubernetes scheduler, KEIDS, and TOPSIS/KCSS. The contribution is architectural and experimental: EcoKube provides a reproducible way to compare sustainability-aware policies before deployment.

</details>


### [8] [STEEL: Sparsity-Aware Fused Attention for Energy-Efficient Long-Sequence Inference on AMD's XDNA NPU](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09385)
*Victor J. B. Jung,Gagandeep Singh,Joseph Melber,Kristof Denolf,Francesco Conti,Luca Benini*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文提出STEEL，首个针对XDNA类NPU的开源FlashAttention实现。通过高效数据流设计、空间并行性和稀疏性感知的流水线放置，在AMD Ryzen AI 9 HX 370 SoC上相比CPU和GPU分别降低能耗9.17倍和1.75倍，并在XDNA 1上实现9.6倍延迟降低。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型代理在操作系统中的广泛采用，笔记本电脑SoC上的能效推理变得愈发重要。云端卸载存在可靠性和隐私问题，而现有NPU由于架构多样性和显式数据移动编程模型，难以有效映射注意力机制。

Method: 提出STEEL框架：（1）针对prefill注意力设计数据流公式，高效利用空间并行性和片上内存；（2）利用稀疏性感知的流水线放置在NPU阵列上处理因果掩码导致的负载不均衡，减少同步开销，提高利用率。

Result: 在AMD Ryzen AI 9 HX 370 SoC上，STEEL相比CPU和GPU基线分别降低能耗9.17倍和1.75倍。在XDNA 1上相比先前最优方案实现9.6倍延迟降低，在XDNA 2上相比逐层注意力实现22.8倍加速。

Conclusion: STEEL有效证明了在笔记本电脑NPU上高效实现注意力机制的可行性，为未来端侧大模型代理的能效推理提供了开源基础方案。

Abstract: The growing adoption of large language model-based agents within operating system workflows has increased the importance of energy-efficient inference on laptop-class systems-on-chip (SoCs). While cloud offloading remains common, it introduces reliability and privacy concerns that are particularly problematic for agentic workloads. Recent laptop SoCs, therefore, incorporate neural processing engines (NPUs) optimized for energy efficiency; however, effectively mapping attention mechanisms onto NPUs remains challenging due to architectural diversity and explicit data-movement programming models. In this work, we present STEEL, the first open-source implementation of FlashAttention targeting XDNA-like NPUs. STEEL introduces a dataflow formulation of prefill attention, enabling efficient exploitation of spatial parallelism and on-chip memory. Furthermore, STEEL addresses the load imbalance induced by the causal mask by leveraging a sparsity-aware pipeline placement onto the NPU array, reducing synchronization overhead and improving utilization. We evaluate STEEL on the AMD Ryzen AI 9 HX 370 SoC and compare its performance against optimized CPU and GPU implementations. Experimental results show that STEEL reduces energy consumption by an average of 9.17x and 1.75x relative to CPU and GPU baselines, respectively. On XDNA 1, STEEL achieves an average 9.6x latency reduction over the prior state of the art, and delivers a 22.8x speedup on average compared to a layer-by-layer attention implementation on XDNA 2.

</details>


### [9] [Short Graph Sketches Suffice for Error-resilient Leader Verification in CONGEST](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09522)
*Pawel Garncarek,Tomasz Jurdziński,Dariusz Kowalski,Subhajit Pramanick*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文研究了CONGEST模型下的局部可验证证明（LCPE）问题，针对树结构上的唯一领导者验证问题，提出了基于局部图草图、想象树和想象认证的方法，仅需O(ε²log n)比特和O(ε²)轮通信即可容忍最多ε个恶意证书错误，并给出了匹配的不可能性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的LCPE算法基于LOCAL模型设计，其无限制的通信能力使其无法直接应用于带宽受限的CONGEST模型。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究CONGEST模型下高效的LCPE实现。

Method: 提出局部图草图（local graph sketches）、想象树（imagined trees）和想象认证（imagined certifications）三个核心概念，将验证所需信息压缩为O(ε²log n)比特，设计O(ε²)轮通信的CONGEST算法。

Result: 实现了容忍最多ε个恶意证书错误的LCPE算法，通信复杂度为O(ε²)轮，每个节点仅需O(ε²log n)比特。

Conclusion: 证明了即使在更强大的LOCAL模型下，视图距离不超过ε的验证方案无法容忍ε个证书错误，表明本文算法在视图距离方面的下界是紧的。

Abstract: Locally Checkable Proofs (LCPs) enable the verification of global graph properties using locally checkable certificates assigned by a prover. Recently, this framework was extended to Locally Checkable Proofs-with-Errors (LCPE), where an adversary may corrupt some certificates. Existing LCPE algorithms, however, are designed for the LOCAL model, whose unbounded communication makes them unsuitable for direct implementation in the bandwidth-restricted CONGEST model.
  We initiate the study of efficient CONGEST implementations of LCPE through the \textsc{unique-leader} verification problem on trees. The main challenge is that tolerating $\varepsilon$ certificate errors requires each node to reason about its $(2\varepsilon+1)$-hop neighborhood, whose exact topology may require up to $O(Δ^{2\varepsilon+1}\log n)$ bits to communicate. To overcome this bottleneck, we introduce \emph{local graph sketches}, together with the notions of \emph{imagined trees} and \emph{imagined certifications}, which encode precisely the information needed for verification using only $O(\varepsilon^2\log n)$ bits per node. Based on these sketches, we design an LCPE algorithm that tolerates up to $\varepsilon$ adversarial certificate errors and constructs the required sketches in $O(\varepsilon^2)$ communication rounds in the CONGEST model.
  We complement our algorithm with a matching impossibility result: even in the strictly more powerful LOCAL model, and even with unbounded certificate size, no verification scheme with view distance at most $\varepsilon$ can tolerate $\varepsilon$ adversarial certificate errors. Since every CONGEST algorithm can be simulated in LOCAL, this lower bound immediately applies to CONGEST, showing that a view distance exceeding $\varepsilon$ is unavoidable.

### [10] [New Complexity Classes in Locally Checkable Labeling for Local Computation Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09626)
*Sijin Peng*

Main category: cs.DC

TL;DR: 本文通过复杂度分类的视角研究局部计算算法（LCA），针对局部可检查标记（LCL）问题，在VOLUME模型和LCA模型中构造了多种复杂度（Θ(log^k n) 和 Θ̃(n^{p/q})）的新实例，证明这些复杂度可达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解局部计算算法（LCA）的复杂度分类，探究给定复杂度函数 f(n) 是否存在对应LCL问题，填补LCA复杂度谱系的空白。

Method: 通过堆叠 Rosenbaum 和 Suomela (2020) 在VOLUME模型中构造的复杂度为 Θ(log n) 和 Θ̃(n^{1/k}) 的LCL实例，获得更丰富的复杂度层次。

Result: 在VOLUME模型和LCA模型中，构造了复杂度为 Θ(log^k n)（任意正整数 k≥1）和 Θ̃(n^{p/q})（任意有理数 p/q∈(0,1]）的LCL问题。

Conclusion: LCL问题的局部计算复杂度可以覆盖对数多项式和亚线性多项式范围的多种复杂度，且构造方法与分布式LOCAL模型中的已有结果完全不同。

Abstract: Local Computation Algorithms (LCAs), introduced by Rubinfeld, Tamir, Vardi, and Xie (2011), are a special type of sublinear algorithms that, given probing access to a possibly massive input, are required to provide query access to a consistent solution, without maintaining a state between different queries. In this paper, we try to understand LCA through the lens of complexity classifications, described by the following question: Given a target complexity function $f(n)$, is there a problem whose local computation complexity is $f(n)$, up to polylogarithmic factors?
  We restrict our focus to Locally Checkable Labeling (LCL) problems, which can be seen as constant-degree constraint satisfaction problems. Possible complexity classes of this problem family have been extensively studied in various distributed computation models, including the $\mathrm{VOLUME}$ model proposed by Rosenbaum and Suomela (2020), which is an invariant of local computation algorithms with additional locality requirements.
  In this paper, we provide new LCL complexity constructions in the $\mathrm{VOLUME}$ model, and generalize the results to LCAs. Specifically, we show that there are LCLs whose probe complexities in the $\mathrm{VOLUME}$ and LCA models are $Θ(\log^k n)$ and $\tilde Θ(n^{p/q})$ for any positive integer $k \ge 1$ and rational $p/q \in (0,1]$. Our approach, completely different from the approach to a similar result in the distributed $\mathrm{LOCAL}$ model by Balliu et al. (2018), is to stack instances of complexity $Θ(\log n)$ and $\tilde Θ(n^{1/k})$ in the $\mathrm{VOLUME}$ model constructed by Rosenbaum and Suomela (2020).

</details>

### [11] [Improved Error Bounds for Pure Differentially Private Continual Counting via Matrix Factorization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08963)
*Pavel Arkhipov,Nikita P. Kalinin*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对纯差分隐私下的持续计数问题，改进了最大均方误差和均方误差的常数项，提出了一种基于矩阵分解的机制，并在{0,1}矩阵类上证明了匹配的下界Ω(ε⁻²log³n)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持续计数是持续观察模型中最基础的问题之一，但已知上界与下界之间存在渐近差距（上界O(ε⁻²log³n)，下界Ω(ε⁻²log²n)），且现有最优上界的常数仍有改进空间。

Method: 采用通用的矩阵分解机制，首先通过基于梯度的优化获得低维高质量分解，然后构造显式矩阵将该分解扩展到任意高维并进一步提升误差保证，最后给出高效算法实现。

Result: 改进了最大均方误差和均方误差的领先常数；在{0,1}矩阵因子分解类上证明了Ω(ε⁻²log³n)的下界，与该类上的上界渐近匹配。

Conclusion: 本文缩小了纯DP持续计数问题的误差上下界差距，尤其是对{0,1}矩阵类给出了紧界；但将下界推广到任意矩阵分解以及更一般的机制仍是开放问题。

Abstract: Continual counting under pure differential privacy is one of the simplest and most well-studied problems in the continual observation model. Nevertheless, an asymptotic gap remains between the best known upper and lower bounds for maximum squared error and mean squared error: the upper bound is $O(ε^{-2}\log^3 n)$, while the lower bound is $Ω(ε^{-2}\log^2 n)$, for both error metrics. The best known constant in the upper bound is achieved by the $k$-ary tree mechanism with the subtraction trick, due to Andersson, Pagh, Steiner, and Torkamani (FORC 2025). In this work, we improve the leading constant in the maximum squared error and the mean squared error. Our approach uses a general matrix factorization mechanism, yielding an improved bound for pure-DP continual counting that does not rely on a tree-based construction. The mechanism starts from a good-quality low-dimensional factorization, obtained via gradient-based optimization, and gives an explicit matrix construction that lifts this factorization to arbitrarily large dimensions, further improving its error guarantees. We offer an efficient algorithmic implementation of our mechanism. On the lower-bound side, we prove an $Ω(ε^{-2}\log^3 n)$ lower bound for the class of factorizations whose matrices have entries in $\{0,1\}$, matching the upper-bound asymptotics for this class. This class includes the binary tree mechanism and $k$-ary tree mechanisms without the subtraction trick. Extending this lower bound to arbitrary matrix factorizations, and beyond the matrix mechanism altogether, remains an open problem.

### [12] [Improved lower bounds of the time complexity of shellsort](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08997)
*Zhenghan Zang*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文通过参数化映射框架对Shellsort进行运行时分析，证明了使用Tokuda增量序列的Shellsort最坏时间复杂度为Ω(N^{1.26})，并推广到任意严格递减增量序列。同时证明了要达到O(N log^c N)的最坏情况时间复杂度，增量序列需要满足特定的数量要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Shellsort的时间复杂度分析长期存在难题，特别是对Tokuda增量序列（1992年提出）的最坏情况时间复杂度缺乏严格的下界证明。作者希望建立统一的数学框架来系统分析Shellsort的运行时间。

Method: 提出参数化映射 [σ(1), σ(2), ..., σ(n)] → σ(1)z + σ(2)z² + ... + σ(n)zⁿ 作为分析工具。通过对该映射的数学性质研究，推导Shellsort的时间复杂度下界，并将结果推广到一般的严格递减增量序列。

Result: 1. Tokuda增量序列的最坏时间复杂度至少为Ω(N^{1.26})。2. 将上述结果推广到任何严格递减增量序列，其中每个项与有理几何序列的距离不超过固定值。3. 严格递减增量序列若要达到O(N log^c N)的最坏情况时间复杂度，必须包含Ω(log N / log log N)个数量级为Ω(N/(log log N)^c)的项。

Conclusion: Shellsort的时间复杂度下界可以通过参数化映射方法得到更精确的刻画，该框架为理解Shellsort的增量序列选择提供了理论指导。

Abstract: In this paper we develop the framework of using a parametrized mapping $[σ(1), σ(2), \cdots, σ(n)] \mapsto σ(1)z + σ(2)z^2 + \cdots σ(n)z^n$ to perform runtime analysis on Shellsort. In particular, we show that the worst-case time complexity of Shellsort using Tokuda's gap sequence proposed in 1992 is at least $Ω(N^{1.26})$ with a generalisation of this result to any strictly decreasing gap sequence where each term at most a fixed distance away from a rational geometric sequence, and we also show that strictly decreasing gap sequences giving worst-case Shellsort time complexities of $O(N \log^c N)$ must have $Ω(\log N / \log \log N)$ terms of order $Ω(N / (\log \log N)^c)$.

### [13] [Rank-Independent Spectral Hypergraph Sparsification via Global-Dictionary Chaining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09074)
*Chenghua Liu,Yuxin Zhang*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文证明了任意加权超图在n个顶点上存在一个谱ε-稀疏化器，仅需O(n log n / ε²)条超边，消除了先前工作中对秩的依赖，并回答了Lee的公开问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前Lee和Jambulapati等人（STOC 2023）的工作构造的谱超图稀疏化器所需超边数量依赖于秩（rank），Lee提出疑问这种依赖是否是本质的。本文旨在消除秩依赖，回答该公开问题。

Method: 提出全局字典链（global-dictionary chaining）技术：首先选取具有平衡有效电阻的团边权重，使得每条超边的半范数相对于由归一化顶点对方向生成的同一全局字典范数是Lipschitz的；从而用该公共字典的高斯宽度替代了局部秩复杂度。

Result: 得到了与秩无关的O(n log n / ε²)超边数量的谱稀疏化器，该结果优于先前依赖于秩的界，并且由于后续大量谱超图稀疏化工作继承了先前的采样界，本结果自动改进了这些后续工作的理论保证。

Conclusion: 秩依赖并非本质，全局字典链技术可以彻底消除它，为谱超图稀疏化领域提供了更紧的、与秩无关的采样界。

Abstract: We show that every weighted hypergraph on $n$ vertices admits a spectral $\varepsilon$-sparsifier with $O(n\log n/\varepsilon^2)$ hyperedges, strengthening the independent STOC 2023 works of Lee and Jambulapati--Liu--Sidford by removing their rank dependence and answering Lee's open question on whether this loss is inherent. The key idea is global-dictionary chaining: after choosing clique edge weights with balanced effective resistances, every hyperedge seminorm is Lipschitz with respect to the same global-dictionary norm generated by normalized vertex-pair directions; the local rank complexity is thereby replaced by the Gaussian width of this common dictionary. Since these STOC 2023 works have become standard analytic primitives across a broad subsequent literature on spectral hypergraph sparsification and its variants, our rank-independent theorem sharpens many later guarantees that inherit their sampling bounds.

</details>


### [14] [Achieving Almost Exact Recovery in Almost Quadratic Time: Rank-Based Graph Matching via Local Tree Correlation Tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09087)
*Jiale Cheng,Ziao Wang,Lei Ying*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于局部树相关性测试的秩排序图匹配算法，在相关Erdős-Rényi图对模型下，当λ=(log n)^{α+o(1)}（α∈(0,1)）且s∈(√C_Otter,1]时，以n^{2+o(1)}时间复杂度和高概率实现近乎精确匹配，首次在该参数区间达到近二次时间复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图匹配算法在相关ER图模型中，当λ处于亚多项式增长区间时，最佳算法（枝形吊灯计数算法）的时间复杂度c(s)随s接近√C_Otter而趋于无穷，效率低下。本文旨在设计一个在此参数区间内达到近二次复杂度的算法。

Method: 提出基于局部树相关性测试的秩排序算法：1）利用树相关性测试构建顶点对之间的匹配得分；2）采用秩排序机制替代传统阈值规则进行顶点配对，避免计算显式阈值（后者计算困难）；3）通过建立发散度情形下树相关性测试的新理论分析，证明阈值型算法的阈值存在性；4）将秩排序算法与阈值型算法性能耦合，证明近乎精确恢复。

Result: 算法在假设λ=(log n)^{α+o(1)}（α∈(0,1)）和s∈(√C_Otter,1]下，以n^{2+o(1)}时间复杂度实现高概率的近乎精确匹配，是该参数区间首个近二次复杂度算法。

Conclusion: 本文在理论上推进了相关ER图匹配问题的算法效率边界，证明了局部树相关性测试在发散度情形下的有效性，为后续图匹配研究提供了新的分析框架和算法设计思路。

Abstract: This paper studies graph matching under the correlated $\text{Erdős-Rényi}$ (ER) graph pair model. This model first samples an $\mathrm{ER}(n,\fracλ{ns})$ base graph, whose edges are then independently subsampled twice with probability $s$ to produce two correlated $\mathrm{ER}(n,\fracλ{n})$ graphs. We propose a graph matching algorithm that has $n^{2+o(1)}$ time complexity and achieves almost exact recovery with high probability under the assumptions $λ=(\log n)^{α+o(1)}$ for some $α\in(0,1)$ and $s\in(\sqrt{C_{\mathrm{Otter}}},1]$, where $C_{\mathrm{Otter}}\approx 0.338$ is Otter's tree-counting constant. This is the first algorithm with almost quadratic time complexity in this regime of $λ$, while the best known result in this regime is the chandelier-counting algorithm with time complexity $O(n^{c(s)})$, where $c(s)\rightarrow \infty$ as $s$ approaches $\sqrt{C_\mathrm{Otter}}$ from above. The proposed algorithm is based on local tree correlation tests. It uses a rank-based algorithm to match the vertex pairs instead of threshold-based rules in the literature. This avoids the need of computing an explicit threshold, which is computationally difficult to obtain. To prove the almost exact recovery result, we establish a new analysis of tree correlation tests in the diverging-degree regime, where both the mean degree and the tree depth grow with $n$. Based on this new result, we establish the existence of a threshold for a threshold-based graph matching algorithm via local tree correlation tests. Finally, we couple the performance of the rank-based algorithm with the threshold-based algorithm to show almost exact recovery.

</details>


### [15] [Gårding's Theorem for Posynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09168)
*Nima Anari*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文将Gårding定理推广到齐次正项式：若定义在右半平面乘积上的齐次正项式（非负实指数单项式的有限正和）无零点，则其归一化根是凹函数。进而，在角度为απ的扇形区域内无零点意味着α-分数次对数凹性。这一结果强化了固定尺寸匹配和非对称行列式点过程的通用混合与域稀疏性保证。研究过程使用了AI辅助交互，由作者发起并核查；Codex还协助了手稿的整理与排版。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典的Gårding定理（关于多项式零点分布与凹性/对数凹性的联系）从标准多项式推广到更一般的齐次正项式（允许任意非负实指数），以建立更广泛的零点-凹性对应关系。

Method: 理论推广：通过将Gårding定理的证明思路扩展到齐次正项式（单项式指数可为任意非负实数），证明在右半平面乘积上无零点时归一化根的凹性；并进一步推导扇形无零点区域与分数次对数凹性之间的定量联系。

Result: 1) 齐次正项式在右半平面乘积上无零点 ⇒ 归一化根为凹函数；2) 在角度απ的扇形内无零点 ⇒ α-分数次对数凹性；3) 该结果改进了固定尺寸匹配和非对称行列式点过程的混合与域稀疏性保证。

Conclusion: 成功将Gårding定理推广到指数为非负实数的齐次正项式，揭示了更广义的零点分布与凹性/对数凹性之间的内在联系，并为相关概率与组合结构提供了更紧的理论保证。

Abstract: We extend Gårding's theorem to homogeneous posynomials: if a finite positive sum of monomials with arbitrary nonnegative real exponents is zero-free on a product of right half-planes, then its degree-normalized root is concave. Consequently, zero-freeness in a sector of aperture $απ$ implies $α$-fractional log-concavity. This sharpens generic mixing and domain-sparsification guarantees for fixed-size matchings and nonsymmetric determinantal point processes. The result was developed in an AI-assisted interaction initiated and checked by the author; Codex also assisted with assembling and typesetting the manuscript.

### [16] [General Non-Clairvoyant KV-Cache Scheduling via Regime-Aware Routing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09248)
*Yiding Feng,Siyu Liu,Zonghan Yang,Yuhao Zhang*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对大语言模型批处理推理中的非预知调度问题，在硬性KV缓存内存预算约束下，提出了首个常数竞争比的调度算法，不依赖任何额外假设，通过新颖的"区域感知路由框架"结合多个专用子调度器实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM批处理推理中，每个请求的响应长度未知（非预知），但已知提示长度。内存占用包括固定提示部分和随解码增长的响应部分。在有限的KV缓存预算下，如何高效调度请求以最小化总完成时间是一个挑战，现有方法缺乏理论保证。

Method: 提出一个"区域感知路由框架"（regime-aware routing framework）：设计多个专用子调度器，分别处理不同内存增长几何特性；同时有一个元调度器在子调度器之间时分共享内存预算，并根据请求执行过程中逐步展现的行为动态路由每个请求。

Result: 对于任意提示长度和任意响应长度，无需额外假设，首次实现了常数竞争比算法。该框架还进一步保证了makespan（最大完工时间）和在线到达场景下的总完成时间也具有常数竞争比。

Conclusion: 该工作首次为非预知LLM批推理调度问题提供了常数竞争比的理论保证，区域感知路由框架为处理不同内存增长模式提供了灵活而有效的解决方案。

Abstract: We study non-clairvoyant scheduling for batched Large Language Model (LLM) inference under a hard Key-Value (KV) cache memory budget. Each request has a known prompt length but an unknown response length, and its memory footprint comprises a fixed prompt component together with a response component that grows with each decoded token. At each decoding round, the scheduler chooses a feasible batch of active requests; evicting a request discards its accumulated cache states, wasting prior computation. The goal is to minimize total completion time against the optimal clairvoyant schedule that knows all response lengths.
  We present the first constant-competitive algorithm for arbitrary prompt lengths and arbitrary response lengths with no additional assumptions. Rather than relying on a single universal scheduling policy, our algorithm is built on a novel regime-aware routing framework. Specialized sub-schedulers handle different memory-growth geometries, while a meta-scheduler time-shares the memory budget across them and dynamically routes each job as its execution progressively reveals its behavior. This framework also yields constant-competitive guarantees for makespan and for total completion time under online arrivals.

### [17] [Matroid Contention Resolution with Concentration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09268)
*Stephen Arndt,Benjamin Moseley,Kirk Pruhs,Michael Zlatin*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文为随机顺序CRS（AW方法）推导了下尾界，证明每个线性函数能以常数因子逼近期望值，失败概率仅与期望值和拟阵数量有关，与基集大小无关。该结果应用于k-拟阵交集着色问题和带覆盖约束的单调子模最大化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知CRS分析通常只能保证期望值的下界和上尾的集中性，缺乏下尾界的保证，因此难以应用于包含覆盖约束的问题（证明覆盖约束成立需要下尾界）。

Method: 提出了"强λ-有界性"新性质，强化了AW的λ-有界性以提供对传播过程的双侧控制；引入"顺序选择过程"随机过程模型，证明任何强λ-有界顺序选择过程都具备下尾界。

Result: 1) 将k-拟阵交集着色近似比从O(k²)改进至O(k log k)；2) 提出了首个在k个拟阵约束及打包/覆盖约束下单调子模最大化的双准则近似算法。

Conclusion: 通过建立CRS的下尾界，拓展了CRS工具在覆盖约束问题中的应用范围，为涉及覆盖约束的组合优化问题提供了新的理论保证。

Abstract: Contention resolution schemes (CRS) are a fundamental and widely applied tool for rounding fractional solutions subject to combinatorial constraints. However, the known analyses of CRS generally only guarantee lower bounds on the expected value and concentration on the upper tail, but no concentration on the lower tail. Thus, CRS are generally not applicable to problems that contain covering constraints, since certifying a covering constraint holds requires a lower tail bound.
  Our main contribution is to derive lower tail bounds for the output of a particular contention resolution scheme, the random-order CRS of Adamczyk and Włodarczyk, which we call AW. We show that every linear function of the rounded solution attains a constant fraction of its expectation with a failure probability that is dimension-free, depending only on the expected value and on the number of matroids, but not on the size of the ground set.
  Our analysis is driven by a new property we call \emph{strong $λ$-boundedness}, which strengthens the known $λ$-boundedness of AW by providing two-sided control on how rounding propagates between elements. We then introduce a random process capturing AW, a \emph{sequential selection process}, that may be of independent interest. We prove lower tail bounds for any strongly $λ$-bounded sequential selection process.
  To demonstrate the applicability of our new tail bounds, we apply them to two problems involving covering constraints. The first result is an $O(k \log k)$-approximation for $k$-matroid intersection coloring (improving the prior $O(k^2)$) when the chromatic number of at least one matroid is $Ω(k^3 \log n)$, where $n$ is the number of elements. The second is the first bicriteria approximation algorithm for monotone submodular maximization under $k$ matroid constraints together with packing and covering constraints.

</details>


### [18] [Faster Exact Algorithms for Equal-Subset-Sum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09289)
*Ryosuke Yamano,Tetsuo Shibuya*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究 Equal-Subset-Sum 问题，改进了 Randolph 和 Węgrzycki (STOC 2026) 的算法，将时间和空间复杂度从 $O^*(1.7067^n)$ 降至 $O^*(1.6994^n)$ 时间和 $O^*(1.5664^n)$ 空间；同时将多项式空间运行时间从 $O^*(2.6817^n)$ 改进至 $O^*(2.5430^n)$，并探索了时间-空间权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Equal-Subset-Sum 是经典子集和问题的变体，在密码学、组合优化等领域有重要应用。现有算法在时间和空间上仍有改进空间，尤其是时间-空间权衡方面尚未充分探索，因此需要更优的算法。

Method: 通过改进 Randolph 和 Węgrzycki 的算法框架，结合更精细的分治策略和组合优化技术，在指数时间算法中实现更优的常数基底，同时利用时间-空间权衡优化多项式空间算法。

Result: 主要结果是：新算法达到 $O^*(1.6994^n)$ 时间和 $O^*(1.5664^n)$ 空间，优于此前的 $O^*(1.7067^n)$；多项式空间算法从 $O^*(2.6817^n)$ 改进至 $O^*(2.5430^n)$。此外，在多种指数空间约束下均取得运行时间改进。

Conclusion: 本文在 Equal-Subset-Sum 问题的精确算法上取得了新的最优界，尤其在时间-空间权衡方面提供了更全面的改进，为后续研究奠定了新基准。

Abstract: We study exact algorithms for Equal-Subset-Sum in the worst-case setting: given a set $S$ of $n$ integers, find two distinct subsets $A,B\subseteq S$ whose sums are equal. We establish a new state-of-the-art bound for this problem by improving the fastest known algorithm, due to Randolph and Węgrzycki (STOC 2026), from $O^*(1.7067^n)$ time and space to an algorithm that runs in $O^*(1.6994^n)$ time and uses $O^*(1.5664^n)$ space. We also improve the best known polynomial-space running time, due to Mucha, Nederlof, Pawlewicz, and Węgrzycki (ESA 2019), from $O^*(2.6817^n)$ to $O^*(2.5430^n)$. Finally, we investigate time-space tradeoffs for this problem and improve the running times achievable under a broad range of exponential-space bounds.

</details>


### [19] [A Polynomial-Time Algorithm for Coloring Perfect Graphs Based on Walk Counting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09309)
*Amir Ali Ahmadi,Pravesh K. Kothari,Yukai Tang*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图论操作的完美图多项式时间最优着色算法，核心是通过迭代计算图中带权重的游走来判定是否存在指定大小的团。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 完美图是最优着色问题的核心图类，此前已有的多项式时间算法（如Lovász的椭球法）依赖于线性规划和几何方法，缺乏纯粹图论视角的算法。作者希望找到一种完全基于图论操作的完美图着色算法。

Method: 算法通过迭代更新图中边和非边的权重来工作。初始权重采用均匀方案，然后每轮迭代根据前一轮的游走计数更新权重，最终通过这些权重信息判定完美图中是否存在指定大小的团。

Result: 作者证明了该算法能够在多项式时间内判定完美图中是否存在给定大小的团，进而实现最优着色。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个完全基于图论操作的完美图最优着色算法，避免了以往算法对线性规划等几何方法的依赖，丰富了完美图的理论研究。

Abstract: We present a polynomial-time algorithm for optimally coloring perfect graphs that is based entirely on graph-theoretic operations. At its core, the algorithm decides whether a perfect graph contains a clique of a given size by iteratively counting walks in the graph with certain weights assigned to its edges and nonedges. These weights are initialized according to a uniform scheme and then updated in each iteration based on the walk counts from the previous iteration.

</details>


### [20] [Subexponential Algorithm for High Multiplicity Fair Division of Mixed Instances via Stereometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09327)
*Yuriy Dementiev,Fedor Pribytkov,Danil Sagunov*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出首个次指数时间算法，在物品分为三类、agent具有加性估值（可正可负）的情况下，在O((n·m)^{√n})时间内找到无嫉妒分配或报告无解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无嫉妒分配算法要么限于两类物品，要么时间复杂度指数级高。本文希望在更一般的三类物品且估值可正可负的场景下，实现比纯粹指数时间更优的算法。

Method: 利用无嫉妒分配在ℝ³中的凸多面体几何表示，结合Miller平面环分离器定理递归地将agent集合分解为平衡子集，从而设计次指数时间算法。

Result: 实现了运行时间(n·m)^{O(√n)}的次指数时间算法，能判断无嫉妒分配是否存在并给出分配；同时可扩展至部分分配已固定的场景。

Conclusion: 该工作是首个在三类物品（含混合估值）场景下的次指数时间无嫉妒分配算法，为更一般情形的高效算法设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: We study the problem of computing an envy-free (EF) allocation of $m$ indivisible items among $n$ agents when items come in three distinct types. Each agent holds additive valuations over item types that may be positive (goods), negative (chores), or mixed. We present the first subexponential-time algorithm with running time time $(n \cdot m)^{O(\sqrt{n})}$ that finds an EF allocation whenever one exists, or correctly reports that none exists. Our approach exploits a geometric representation of EF allocations as convex polyhedra in $\mathbb{R}^3$ and applies Miller's planar cycle-separator theorem to recursively decompose the agent set into balanced subgroups. We further extend the algorithm to handle agents whose allocations are fixed in advance, preserving envy-freeness across all agents.

### [21] [Spanning Paths and Cycles: Structural Limitations of the Irrelevant Vertex Technique](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09342)
*Dimitrios M. Thilikos,Sebastian Wiederrecht*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了生成路径问题中“无关顶点技术”的适用边界，发现其有效性取决于标注图的深度参数depth_2，并给出了完全的组合二分性刻画：在红-子式封闭类中，该技术适用当且仅当depth_2有界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典无关顶点技术在生成路径问题中表现与经典路由问题不同，其适用性不由区分顶点数量决定，而由顶点分布方式决定。作者希望精确刻画这一现象的本质结构参数。

Method: 引入了标注图的新结构参数depth_2；证明了针对有界depth_2标注图的局部结构定理；建立了生成版本的 Vital Linkage Theorem；基于以上理论设计了时间复杂度为2^{2^{poly(k+d)}}·n^2的算法。

Result: 给出了完全的组合二分性刻画：在红-子式封闭类中，无关顶点技术适用于Spanning Disjoint Paths问题当且仅当该类有有界depth_2。即使在平面图上，超过该边界时无关顶点规则也不存在。

Conclusion: depth_2是无关顶点技术在生成约束下的精确组合障碍，划定了Robertson-Seymour范式在生成路径问题中适用与否的严格结构边界。

Abstract: The Irrelevant Vertex Technique is one of the cornerstones of algorithmic graph theory, underlying Robertson and Seymour's algorithm for \textsc{Disjoint Paths} and much of the algorithmic Graph Minors theory. We show that, in the setting of spanning routing, this technique exhibits an exact combinatorial limitation. Unlike classical routing problems, spanning routing is not governed by the number of distinguished vertices but by the way they are distributed throughout the graph. The input is a triple $(G,R,\mathcal{T})$ where $(G,R)$ is an annotated graph and $\mathcal{T}$ is a set of terminal pairs. The goal is to determine if $G$ contains a family of internally disjoint paths connecting the pairs in $\mathcal{T}$ such that the union of the paths spans the set $R$. We identify a new structural parameter of annotated graphs, called $\mathsf{depth}_2$, that measures precisely this phenomenon. Our main result is a complete combinatorial dichotomy: for every red-minor-closed class of annotated graphs, the Irrelevant Vertex Technique applies to \textsc{Spanning Disjoint Paths} \textsl{if and only if} the class has bounded $\mathsf{depth}_2$. Thus $\mathsf{depth}_2$ forms the exact structural boundary between classes where the Robertson-Seymour paradigm survives and those where it breaks down. Our proof combines a new local structure theorem for annotated graphs of bounded $\mathsf{depth}_2$ with a spanning analogue of the celebrated Vital Linkage Theorem. The resulting algorithm solves \textsc{Spanning Disjoint Paths} in time $2^{2^{\mathbf{poly}(k+d)}}\cdot n^2$ where $d$ is the $\mathsf{depth}_2$ of the input instance. We provide matching lower bounds showing that beyond bounded $\mathsf{depth}_2$ no irrelevant-vertex rule can exist, even on planar graphs. In particular, $\mathsf{depth}_2$ is the exact combinatorial barrier for the Irrelevant Vertex Technique under spanning constraints.

</details>


### [22] [Strong Refutation of Random Ordering CSPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09410)
*Xifan Yu*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机排序约束满足问题（ordering CSP）的强反驳（strongly refuting）可满足性问题。提出了基于Kikuchi方法的多项式时间ε-反驳算法，在子句密度高于$\tildeΩ(n^{d/2}/\varepsilon^2)$时有效，并给出了运行时间、子句密度与反驳强度之间的平滑三维权衡。同时通过低坐标度算法的计算下界证明了该权衡的近似最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机CSP的强反驳是理论计算机科学中的重要问题，但之前对ordering CSP（一种变量为全排列的约束满足问题）的强反驳研究尚属空白。本文旨在填补这一空白，并探索算法效率与反驳强度之间的根本性折中关系。

Method: 利用Kikuchi方法（一种基于高阶矩的谱方法）设计多项式时间ε-反驳算法；通过调整算法参数实现运行时间、子句密度和反驳强度ε之间的三维权衡；采用低坐标度算法模型建立计算下界。

Result: 1) 当子句数$\tildeΩ(n^{d/2}/\varepsilon^2)$时存在多项式时间ε-反驳算法；2) 实现了运行时间、子句密度与反驳强度的连续三维权衡；3) 基于低坐标度算法的下界表明该权衡接近最优。

Conclusion: 本文首次将强反驳研究拓展到ordering CSP领域，所提出的三维权衡框架在低坐标度算法模型下近乎最优，为理解随机ordering CSP的算法极限提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this work, we initiate the study of strongly refuting the satisfiability of random ordering constraint satisfaction problems. We show that there is a polynomial-time $\varepsilon$-refutation algorithm for random ordering CSP with predicate $P$ when the number of clauses is above the threshold $\tildeΩ\left(n^{d/2}/\varepsilon^2\right)$, where $d$ is the coordinate degree of the predicate $P$. We further give a smooth three-way tradeoff between the running time, the clause density, and the refutation strength $\varepsilon$ using the Kikuchi method. Finally, we complement our algorithmic results with a computational lower bound based on the class of low coordinate degree algorithms, providing evidence that the established three-way tradeoff is near optimal.

</details>


### [23] [A combinatorial framework for clustering graph states: Algorithms and hardness for rank-integrity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09469)
*Romain Bourneuf,Nathan Claudet,Sang Yoon Kim,Rose McCarty,Blair D. Sullivan,Stéphan Thomassé*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于图态距离的新框架，通过辅助量子比特数度量两个图态之间的"距离"，并利用顶点子图理论给出其图形化描述。在此框架下定义了"辅助完整性"问题，证明其与秩完整性问题的等价性（辅助量子比特数最多差2倍），并分析了秩完整性的参数复杂度（XP可解于参数k，但W[1]-难），同时给出了k=1时的O(n^6)算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图态是量子信息处理中的重要资源，但如何量化不同图态之间的"接近程度"并识别图态中的"高纠缠簇"缺乏系统理论。本文旨在建立一种基于最少辅助量子比特数的图态距离度量，并利用图论中的顶点子图理论为量子网络中的编辑距离问题提供经典算法工具。

Method: 提出图态间距离定义为所需最少辅助量子比特数（允许使用单量子比特Clifford门、Pauli测量和经典通信）。通过顶点子图（vertex-minors）的透镜给出该距离的图形化描述。将辅助完整性问题转化为秩完整性问题（GF(2)上邻接矩阵和的秩），并采用参数复杂度理论进行分析。

Result: 证明辅助完整性与秩完整性在因子2内等价。秩完整性在参数k下是XP可解的，同时也是W[1]-难的。对于k=1的情况，给出了显式的O(n^6)算法。

Conclusion: 本文建立了图态距离的形式化理论，为量子网络中的图编辑距离问题提供了经典算法框架。复杂度结果表明该问题在参数化视角下具有层次性（XP可解但W[1]-难），为后续近似算法或启发式算法的发展提供了理论边界。

Abstract: We introduce a new notion of distance between two graph states $|G\rangle$ and $|G'\rangle$ on the same set of qubits. This distance is the minimum number of ancilla qubits in a graph state $|\widehat{G}\rangle$ from which both $|G\rangle$ and $|G'\rangle$ can be ``easily prepared''. (When preparing graph states, we are only allowed to use one-qubit Clifford gates, one-qubit Pauli measurements, and classical communication.) We give a graphical description of this distance through the lens of vertex-minors. We then show how this distance yields quantum network analogs of many graph edit-distance problems.
  Using this framework, we develop classical algorithms for identifying the ``highly entangled clusters'' of a graph state $|G\rangle$. The ancilla integrity problem asks, given a graph $G$ and integer $k$, for the minimum -- over all graph states $|G'\rangle$ with distance at most $k$ from $|G\rangle$ -- of the maximum component size of $G'$. Up to a factor of $2$ in the number of ancilla qubits, this problem is equivalent to rank integrity, where the distance between $G$ and $G'$ is instead the minimum rank of the sum of their adjacency matrices over $\text{GF}(2)$. We prove that rank integrity is XP parameterized by $k$. We also prove the complementary hardness result that rank integrity is W[1]-hard in $k$. Finally, we give an explicit $\mathcal{O}(n^6)$-time algorithm for ancilla integrity when $G$ has $n$ vertices and $k=1$.

</details>


### [24] [Streaming with Catalytic Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09475)
*Tamara Kaplan,Nimrod Kaplan,Haim Kaplan*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合催化内存和常规内存的流式计算模型，能够精确计算频率矩和任意多项式，并应用于不同元素计数、三角形计数和重击者识别等任务。同时证明了催化内存在单遍流算法中无用，并展示了在特定限制下打破三遍下界的两遍算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统流式算法通常只能近似计算结果，作者希望利用催化内存（除了常规内存外额外的大容量辅助内存，其初始状态已知且最终状态可被破坏）来实现精确的流式计算，并探索催化内存在流式模型中的能力边界。

Method: 1) 设计使用对数级别常规内存和多项式级别催化内存的流式算法，精确计算频率矩和任意多项式；2) 将流式模型归约到催化通信模型，证明催化内存在单遍算法中无用；3) 通过限制性分析证明某些自然条件下二阶矩至少需要三遍，然后设计两遍算法突破该下界。

Result: 实现了频率矩的常数遍精确计算，以及多项式评估的（度数+1）遍算法。证明了催化内存在单遍流算法中无效，并在特定限制下证明二阶矩至少需三遍，但最终设计了可突破该下界的两遍算法。

Conclusion: 催化内存在多遍流式算法中具有实用价值，能实现精确计算；但单遍情况下无用。这项工作为流式计算提供了新的理论工具，并为未来算法设计提供了指导。

Abstract: We introduce a streaming model that uses both catalytic and regular memory. In this model, we show how to exactly compute the frequency moments using a logarithmic number of bits of regular memory and a polynomial number of bits of catalytic memory. More generally, we show how to compute arbitrary polynomials of the item frequencies exactly within the same space bounds. As an application, we obtain catalytic streaming algorithms that exactly compute the number of distinct elements in a stream, count the number of triangles (or any other small subgraph) in a graph whose edges arrive in a stream, and identify heavy hitters.
  Our algorithms for frequency moments perform a constant number of passes over the stream, and for polynomial evaluation, we require one more pass than the degree of the polynomial.
  By relating our catalytic streaming model to the catalytic communication model introduced in Pyne et al., we show that catalytic memory is not useful for any one-pass streaming algorithm. For lower bounds on multipass streaming algorithms, the impossibility results of Pyne et al. are not strong enough. However, using a different technique, we show that under certain natural restrictions, no catalytic streaming algorithm can compute the second frequency moment in fewer than three passes.
  This definition of the restricted class of two-pass algorithms then guides us in the design of a two-pass algorithm for computing the second moment exactly that circumvents these restrictions and breaks the three-pass barrier.

### [25] [Terminal Dimension Reduction for Time Series with Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09490)
*Alexander Munteanu,Matteo Russo,David Saulpic,Chris Schwiegelshohn*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种推广的终端嵌入方法，能够保持仿射线段的距离，并将其应用于Fréchet距离下的时间序列聚类，首次实现了无维度依赖的coreset构建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的终端嵌入技术无法处理时间序列这类带有线性插值结构的复杂数据，因为终端嵌入是非线性的，无法保持线性结构（如线段）的距离。

Method: 提出了一种针对仿射线段的终端嵌入推广，使其能够保持线段间的距离；结合Johnson-Lindenstrauss嵌入，用于Fréchet距离下的时间序列聚类coreset构建。

Result: 首次获得了Fréchet距离下时间序列聚类的无维度依赖coreset；实验表明终端嵌入与JL性能相当，优于PCA，且只有终端嵌入能将成对距离保持扩展到整个空间。

Conclusion: 推广后的终端嵌入有效解决了线性结构保持问题，为时间序列聚类等复杂结构数据提供了新的降维与coreset工具。

Abstract: Terminal embeddings have emerged as a powerful tool for dimension reduction. Given a set of points $P\subset \mathbb{R}^d$, a terminal embedding is a mapping $f:\mathbb{R}^d\rightarrow \mathbb{R}^t$ that preserves the pairwise distance between any pair of points $p\in P$ and $q\in \mathbb{R}^d$ up to small distortion under this mapping. Terminal embeddings have been particularly fruitful for constructing $k$-means and $k$-median coresets, where the objective is to find a typically weighted subset $Ω$ of $P$ such that for any candidate solution, the cost of the clustering objective on $Ω$ approximates the cost of the clustering objective on $P$ up to small distortion. Unfortunately, these techniques have not been extended to more complicated structures such as clustering time-series data under common straight-line interpolation between measurements. The main issue is that terminal embeddings, arguably the central technique in this line of research, cannot be linear and are thus not immediately suitable to preserve linear structures. In this work, we develop a generalization of terminal embeddings to affine line-segments that overcomes this issue. We showcase their applicability by using our lines-preserving terminal embeddings to obtain the first dimension-free coresets for clustering time-series under the Fréchet distance. The underlying dimension reduction uses Johnson-Lindenstrauss (JL) embeddings, and our experiments indicate that terminal embeddings perform similarly to JL and favorably against PCA for synthetic and real-world time-series, while only terminal embeddings extend pairwise distance preservation to the full ambient space.

</details>


### [26] [Improved Approximation of Min-Distances in Near-Linear Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09588)
*Yael Kirkpatrick*

Main category: cs.DS

TL;DR: 本文针对有向图的最小距离直径近似问题，提出了一个随机化的近线性时间算法，实现了3-近似，超越了此前所有已知的近似-运行时间权衡结果，并进一步将技术扩展到多模态图，在近线性时间内实现了3-近似，大幅改进此前n-近似的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 最小距离（min-distance）不是度量，导致经典技术不适用；此前虽有近似结果（4k-1近似或4-近似），但仍有改进空间。本文希望获得更优的近似比（3-近似），并推广到更一般的多模态图设置。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的"类型分类"（type-classification）框架，将节点分类后分别处理，从而在近线性时间内实现3-近似算法。该框架可能具有独立的研究价值。

Result: 1) 对标准有向图的最小距离直径，实现了3-近似，运行时间为近线性；2) 对2-模态图（multimode graphs）的直径，同样实现了3-近似，大幅优于此前最优的n-近似。

Conclusion: 本文显著缩小了最小距离与多模态距离近似之间的差距，为理解非度量距离测度下的图参数开辟了新方向。

Abstract: We study the problem of approximating the diameter of directed graphs under the min-distance measure, defined as $d_{\min}(u,v) = \min(d(u,v), d(v,u))$. Unlike standard shortest-path distance, min-distance is not a metric, which renders many classical techniques inapplicable. Prior work has therefore focused on approximating this parameter, culminating in an approximation-runtime tradeoff by Dalirrooyfard et al. [ICALP'19] giving a $4k-1$ approximation in $\tilde{O}(mn^{1/(k+1)})$ time for any positive integer $k$ and, more recently, the first near-linear time constant approximation by Chechik and Zhang [FOCS'22], where they obtained a 4-approximation to the min-diameter.
  In this work we present a randomized near-linear time algorithm that achieves a $3$-approximation to the min-diameter, outperforming all known approximation-runtime tradeoffs. Our approach introduces a novel type-classification framework that may be of independent interest.
  We further extend our techniques to the more general setting of multimode graphs, recently introduced as a generalization of min-distance by Kirkpatrick and Vassilevska W. [MFCS'25]. For directed $2$-mode graphs, we obtain a $3$-approximation to the diameter in near-linear time, dramatically improving over the previously best known $n$-approximation. Our results significantly narrow the gap between min-distance and multimode distance approximations, and open new directions for understanding graph parameters under non-metric distance measures.

</details>

### [27] [Programmers Are Poor and Overconfident Judges of LLM-Generated Assertions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08885)
*Zhanna Kaufman,Yuriy Brun,Adithya Murali,Madeline Endres*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验发现，程序员在判断正确断言时准确率尚可（74%），但判断错误断言时表现较差（49%）。自然语言解释对整体评估无帮助，低质量解释甚至会降低评估准确性并增加开发者信心。这表明AI辅助可能不会提高代码理解和审查的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码理解和代码审查是至关重要的软件工程任务，随着AI代码生成工具的普及，这些任务的重要性进一步提升。生成式AI有望通过添加断言和自然语言解释来辅助这些活动，但这类支持的实际效果尚不明确。

Method: 对86名Python程序员进行受控实验，并开展后续的有声思维（think-aloud）研究，考察开发者评估不同质量断言的正确性和完整性的能力，以及自然语言解释如何影响这些评估。

Result: 程序员判断正确断言的准确率为74%，但判断错误断言的准确率仅为49%，两者差异显著（p<0.001），正确断言的判断准确率是错误断言的近3倍（OR=2.94）。自然语言解释未带来整体收益，低质量解释反而降低了评估准确性（p=0.037, OR=0.58）并增加了开发者信心（p=0.005）。

Conclusion: 与普遍假设相反，AI辅助可能并不会提高代码理解和审查的可靠性。研究结果强调，除了生成可靠性工件外，帮助开发者评估这些机器生成的可靠性工件同样重要。

Abstract: Code comprehension and code review are already critically important software engineering tasks, and the rising use of AI code generation tools is only increasing that importance. Generative AI has the possibility of supporting these activities, for example by augmenting code with assertions and natural-language explanations describing code behavior. However, little is known about how effective such support may be. We conduct a controlled experiment with 86 Python programmers and a follow-up think-aloud study to examine developers' ability to assess the correctness and completeness of generated assertions of varying quality, and to investigate how natural-language explanations influence these assessments. While programmers can somewhat accurately judge correct assertions (74% accuracy), they perform poorly when shown incorrect assertions (49% accuracy), despite reporting similar levels of confidence in both judgments. This difference in judgment accuracy is statistically significant (p < 0.001): the odds of a developer accurately judging a correct assertion was nearly three times higher than the odds of accurately judging an incorrect assertion (OR = 2.94). Surprisingly, natural-language explanations of assertions provided no overall benefit. Furthermore, low-quality explanations could impair specification assessment accuracy (p = 0.037, OR = 0.58) while simultaneously increasing developer confidence (p = 0.005, 3.99/5 vs. 4.25/5). Our findings suggest that, contrary to common assumptions, AI assistance may not improve the reliability of code comprehension and review. More broadly, our findings highlight the importance of helping developers evaluate machine-generated reliability artifacts, in addition to generating them.

</details>


### [28] [Better Harnesses, Smaller Models: Building 90% Cheaper Agents via Automated Harness Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08938)
*Chenyang Yang,Xinran Zhao,Tongshuang Wu,Christian Kästner*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出通过自动化的"工具适配"（harness adaptation）来提升小型语言模型（SLM）在常规商业任务中的表现，使SLM智能体在仅花费LLM 4%-10%成本的情况下，达到接近甚至匹配LLM的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体虽然能力强但推理成本高昂，大规模部署不可持续；SLM成本低但直接替代LLM使用时性能不足。因此需要为SLM定制适配方案，以低成本实现可比的商业任务表现。

Method: 构建了一个系统性框架：1）将智能体失败模式映射到适配策略；2）设计了一个元智能体（harness optimizer），利用失败轨迹自动发现有效的适配方案（包括定制指令、工具和编排循环）。

Result: 在7个商业任务和3个SLM家族上，优化后的适配方案显著提升了16/21个任务-SLM组合的性能，其中7个组合缩小了SLM与LLM的差距，最佳SLM智能体以4%的成本恢复了89.7%的LLM性能。

Conclusion: 适配方案对于工作流重复性高的任务以及基础能力足够的SLM效果最好，表明工具适配可以有效扩展SLM智能体在常规商业任务中的实际部署范围。

Abstract: Frontier LLM agents are automating many business tasks, but their high inference cost makes large-scale deployment unsustainable. Small language models (SLMs) offer a cheaper alternative, yet they typically fall short when swapped into a harness designed for a frontier LLM. We show that for many routine business tasks, SLM agents can match LLM performance at 90% lower cost, when paired with an adapted harness that can be automatically discovered by a meta agent. The key insight is that much of the task difficulty is shared across instances and can be lifted from the model into the harness via tailored instructions, tools, and orchestration loops. To study this systematically, we create a framework that maps agent failure modes to harness adaptation strategies, and build a harness optimizer that automatically discovers effective adaptations from failure trajectories. Across seven business-oriented agentic tasks and three SLM families, we found optimized harnesses significantly improve performance on 16 of 21 task-SLM pairs, with seven pairs closing the SLM-LLM performance gap and the best SLM agent recovering 89.7% of LLM performance at 4% of the cost. Our analysis further shows that adaptation works best for tasks with more repetitive workflows and for SLMs with sufficient base capabilities. Together, these results suggest that harness adaptation can expand the practical deployment range of SLM agents in routine business tasks.

</details>


### [29] [Toward Inferring Accurate Context-free Grammars for Big Languages in a Black-box Setting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08959)
*Mohammad Rifat Arefin,Nuhiat Arefin,Shanto Rahman,Christoph Csallner*

TL;DR: Xvada是一种新的上下文无关文法推断方法，相比现有方法在准确性和紧凑性上更优，并在Python Liquid引擎中发现了一个CVE和五个bug。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑盒上下文无关文法推断方法（如Arvada, TreeVada, Kedavra, Cucio）在大规模语言上存在可扩展性差、准确率低和文法可读性不佳的问题。

Method: Xvada引入了多项新技术，用于确定性推断上下文无关文法。

Result: 在避免近期研究陷阱的实证比较中，Xvada在文法准确性和紧凑性上均优于最佳竞争对手TreeVada；在Python Liquid引擎中发现一个CVE，并通过基于Xvada推断文法的模糊测试发现了5个额外bug。

Conclusion: Xvada在文法推断的准确性和紧凑性上取得了SOTA，且具备实际应用价值（发现真实漏洞），代码和数据已开源。

Abstract: Black-box context-free grammar inference is crucial for program analysis, reverse engineering, program understanding, fuzzing, and security. But existing approaches such as Arvada, TreeVada, Kedavra, and Cucio struggle with scalability, accuracy, and grammar readability, especially on larger languages. To address this challenge, Xvada introduces several new techniques for deterministic inference of context-free grammars. In an empirical comparison that avoids several pitfalls of recent studies, Xvada improves on the highest-scoring competitor (TreeVada) both in grammar accuracy and grammar compactness. Xvada also found a CVE in the widely used Python Liquid engine. Fuzzing based on the XVada-inferred grammar found five more bugs, which the Python Liquid developers fixed based on our bug reports. XVADA and all experimental data and scripts are freely available.

### [30] [The Patchwork Problem in LLM-Generated Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08981)
*Viraaji Mothukuri,Reza M. Parizi*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: LLM生成的代码常因结构性（而非逻辑性）缺陷在部署后崩溃，如引用未声明配置、导入不存在包、遗漏认证守卫等。本文将其定义为"拼布问题"，通过图表示形式化结构一致性，提出八类故障分类法及混合验证框架，实验表明大多数结构缺陷会逃过类型检查、测试和SAST。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM生成代码在单元层面看似正确（编译通过、测试通过），但部署后因结构性不一致而崩溃。标准CI工具链几乎无法发现这类缺陷，随着LLM编码工具普及，这一问题对软件质量构成严重风险。

Method: 将结构一致性形式化为仓库工件的图表示（导入图、调用图、依赖图、配置图、模式图、资源图、控制流图、路由图）上的一致性不变量；提出八类故障分类法；构建混合验证框架，对已有成熟静态分析工具的部分委派给它们，对跨切面不变量开发专用检测器。

Result: 两类前沿模型在四种提示策略下的大量结构缺陷逃过了类型检查、测试和SAST；不同模型的故障模式存在定性差异，挑战了模型无关的缓解策略；在真实世界AI生成仓库上的外部验证证实这些缺陷普遍存在。

Conclusion: LLM生成代码中的结构性缺陷是真实且系统性的问题，现有验证手段严重不足，需要针对结构一致性的专项检测方法。

Abstract: LLM-generated code often compiles, passes tests, and appears correct, yet breaks once deployed. The root cause is frequently structural rather than logical. A generated endpoint references configuration keys never declared in the project, an import targets a package that does not exist in any registry, or a new route omits the authentication guard applied to every sibling endpoint. Each patch is locally valid but globally incoherent, and standard CI toolchains rarely surface these failures. As LLM-powered coding tools see widespread adoption, this blind spot poses a growing risk to software quality. We call this the \textbf{patchwork problem}. This paper formalizes structural coherence as consistency invariants over graph representations of repository artifacts, including import, call, dependency, configuration, schema, resource, control-flow, and routing graphs, and introduces an eight-category failure taxonomy distinguishing defects specific to LLM generation from those merely amplified by it. We present a hybrid verification framework that delegates to mature static analysis tools where they already excel and deploys purpose-built detectors for cross-cutting invariants underserved by existing toolchains, targeting provable constraint violations rather than heuristic pattern matching. Empirical evaluation across two frontier models under four prompting strategies reveals that the vast majority of structural failures evade type checking, testing, and SAST entirely, and that failure patterns diverge qualitatively between models in ways that challenge model-agnostic mitigation strategies. External validation on real-world AI-generated repositories confirms that these failures are not artifacts of controlled experimentation but are prevalent wherever LLMs write code with minimal human oversight.

</details>


### [31] [SCATE: Learning to Supervise Coding Agents for Cost-Effective Test Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08983)
*Sijia Gu,Noor Nashid,Ali Mesbah*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: SCATE是一个自适应自动化监督框架，通过将监督建模为上下文赌博问题，替代人工介入来防止自动化测试生成中的提前终止和懒生成问题，显著提升了代码覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前自动化编码代理在测试生成中存在"懒生成"问题——代理会过早终止任务、系统性地回避复杂程序逻辑，导致代码覆盖不足。现有的缓解方案需要持续的人工监督，形成瓶颈，抵消了自动化生成的效率优势。

Method: 将监督问题形式化为上下文赌博机问题，SCATE学习根据当前覆盖率和类可测试性指标选择最有前景的测试动作，在最大化覆盖率增益的同时最小化无效生成开销。

Result: 与GEMINI-CLI结合时，行覆盖率提升32.3%，分支覆盖率提升30.9%；与CLAUDE CODE对比验证了框架能动态调整策略以优化各代理的独特优势；在所有指标上持续优于现有非代理方法。

Conclusion: SCATE能够无缝集成不同编码代理，用自动化监督替代人工干预，有效解决懒生成问题，是提升自动化测试生成效率和覆盖率的有效框架。

Abstract: While autonomous coding agents have significantly advanced automated test generation, they remain fundamentally limited by lazy generation, a phenomenon where agents prematurely terminate tasks and systematically avoid complex programmatic logic, resulting in inadequate code coverage. Currently, mitigating this premature termination requires continuous human-in-the-loop supervision. This heavy reliance on human intuition creates a bottleneck that negates the efficiency gains of automated generation. We propose SCATE, a framework for adaptive, automated supervision of coding agents that replaces human intervention during test generation. By formulating supervision as a contextual bandit problem, SCATE learns to select the most promising testing actions based on the current coverage and class testability metrics, maximizing coverage gains while minimizing wasted generation effort. Our empirical evaluation demonstrates that SCATE integrates seamlessly with different coding agents. When applied to GEMINI-CLI, it achieves 32.3% higher line coverage and 30.9% higher branch coverage than the agent-only baseline. A comparison with CLAUDE CODE confirms the framework dynamically adapts its policy to optimize each agent's unique strengths. SCATE also consistently outperforms state-of-the-art non-agentic approaches across all metrics.

</details>


### [32] [Loop-Based Slicing and Input-Driven Concretization: An Empirical Study of Termination and Non-Termination Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08988)
*Negar Fathi,Rahul Purandare,Tachio Terauchi,Hiroshi Unno*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了轻量级、工具无关的源码预处理方法（循环切片和输入具体化）对C程序（非）终止性分析的影响，实验证明预处理并非普遍有益，其效果取决于分析器、任务和程序特征，建议作为原程序分析的补充手段自适应使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实C程序中的循环交互和非确定性输入使得现有分析器难以准确验证终止性与非终止性，需要探究轻量级预处理方法能否提升分析效果。

Method: 开发了FocusTNT前端，实现基于循环的切片（隔离循环级义务）和输入驱动具体化（将非确定性输入转化为特定输入场景变体），在117个C/C++真实程序上对6种分析器进行实验评估。

Result: 预处理并非一致有益：切片提供保守的结构隔离和定位，具体化可提升特定场景的可检测性但缩小语义范围并可能增加分析开销，两者组合并不总是叠加效果。

Conclusion: 预处理应作为原程序分析的补充手段自适应使用，为应用开发者理解验证结果和工具开发者改进分析器鲁棒性提供了实践指导。

Abstract: Termination and non-termination are fundamental correctness properties, but verifying them in real-world C programs remains difficult because loop interactions and nondeterministic inputs challenge existing analyzers. This paper presents an empirical study of lightweight, tool-independent source-level preprocessing for (non-)termination analysis. We implement FocusTNT, a C front end that applies loop-based slicing to isolate loop-level obligations and input-driven concretization to specialize nondeterministic inputs into selected input-scenario variants. We evaluate slicing, concretization, and their combination across six analyzers on 117 C/C++ programs derived from real-world non-termination bugs and their fixes. The study examines effects on analyzer correctness, complementarity with original-program analysis, loop-level diagnostics, feature sensitivity, runtime behavior, semantic scope, and integration potential. Results show that preprocessing is not uniformly beneficial: its impact depends on the analyzer, task, and program features. Slicing provides conservative structural isolation and localization, whereas concretization can improve detectability for selected scenarios but narrows semantic scope and may increase analysis effort. Their combination is not consistently additive. Overall, the results support adaptive use of preprocessing as a complement to original-program analysis and provide practical guidance to application developers interpreting verification outcomes and tool developers improving analyzer robustness.

</details>

Result: 不同问题解决风格、经验水平和角色的开发者对审查解释风格的偏好存在差异；整体上，开发者更看重解释深度、学习支持、实用建议和风险意识，而非简洁性。

We report initial findings from an ongoing mixed-methods user study in which developers evaluated persona-aligned review comments across multiple code snippets. Our results suggest that preferences for explanation styles vary across problem-solving styles, experience levels, and roles. Across problem-solving style profiles, developers valued explanatory depth, learning support, practical suggestions, and risk awareness over conciseness, highlighting the need to balance personalization with clarity and trust. Based on these findings, we outline a vision for inclusive, human-centered AI-assisted code review systems that adapt feedback to developers' problem-solving preferences.

### [34] [Shadow-Based Noise Fingerprinting of Simulated Quantum Noise Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08998)
*Vridhi Jain,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合经典影子层析与物理信息特征工程的噪声指纹识别框架，在3量子比特探针电路上，利用279维特征向量和随机森林分类器，对10种噪声类型实现84.26%的分类准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有噪声分类方法（如量子过程层析）随系统规模指数扩展，难以用于近期的量子处理器日常校准。因此需要一种可扩展的噪声识别方法。

Method: 结合结构化经典影子层析（randomized Pauli measurements）与物理信息特征工程，从3量子比特探针电路中提取279维特征向量；分别使用随机森林、极端随机树和多层感知机三种分类器进行训练与评估。

Result: 在包含14000个标注样本、10种噪声类型的数据集上，随机森林分类器取得最高测试准确率0.8426，宏F1得分0.8437，优于其他基线模型。混淆分析显示多数噪声类型可被高可靠识别，混淆主要发生在具有相似物理衰减机制的通道之间。

Conclusion: 该方法可扩展、实用，适用于近期的量子处理器噪声校准。未来工作可探索更丰富的探针态和噪声参数估计，以进一步区分物理机制相似的噪声通道。

Abstract: Accurate noise classification is essential for operating near-term quantum processors, yet existing approaches, such as quantum process tomography, scale exponentially with system size, limiting their practicality for routine calibration. We propose a scalable noise fingerprinting pipeline that combines structured classical shadow tomography with physics-informed feature engineering to identify noise channels from a fixed set of 3-qubit probe circuits. Each sample is represented by a 279-dimensional feature vector constructed from randomized Pauli measurements and derived observables, designed to resolve physically similar noise channels that produce overlapping signatures under generic measurement sets. We evaluate three classifiers, i.e., random forest, extra trees, and a multilayer perceptron, on a dataset of 14,000 labeled samples spanning 10 noise types. The random forest classifier achieves the highest test accuracy of 0.8426 with a macro F1 score of 0.8437, outperforming both baselines. Confusion analysis reveals that many noise types are classified with high reliability, with the remaining confusions occurring between channels sharing similar physical decay mechanisms, motivating future work on richer probe states and noise parameter estimation.

</details>


### [35] [Benchmarking Large Language Models on Repairing Qiskit Programs using Bugs4Q](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09007)
*Saumya Brahmbhatt,Mitali Hukkeri,Dongchan Kim,M. V. Panduranga Rao,Lei Zhang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文发现量子程序基准测试Bugs4Q存在"无声标签反转"问题：当参考修复失效或错误程序不再复现时，基准条目会静默失效。通过跨6个Qiskit版本重新评估67个真实缺陷，发现基准正确性取决于（基准，版本）组合。评估4种LLM的修复能力，GPT-5.4最佳（pass@10 = 48.8%），且大多数修复失败源于API弃用而非错误修复。研究发布重新验证的版本固定基准，强调基准验证必须先于修复评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子程序基准测试Bugs4Q假设其标签始终有效，且生成的修复能在目标环境执行。然而，随着Qiskit版本更新，基准条目可能无声失效，影响修复评估的准确性。作者旨在揭示这一问题并重新验证基准。

Method: 选取两个包含67个唯一真实Qiskit缺陷的Bugs4Q版本，补充缺失的可执行测试，在6个固定Qiskit版本（0.25.0至2.3.1）上重新运行所有条目。评估4种LLM（GPT-4o-mini至GPT-5.4）的修复能力，每个缺陷生成最多10个候选修复，并跨版本测试。

Result: 发现量子基准存在"无声标签反转"问题。GPT-5.4 pass@10最高（48.8%），其次GPT-5.4-mini（47.3%）、GPT-5o-mini（30.3%）、GPT-4o-mini（22.6%）。所有模型在Qiskit 0.45.0表现最佳，在Qiskit 1.0过渡后下降。64%成功修复发生在目标版本下无效的条目上。

Conclusion: 基准正确性依赖于（基准，版本）组合而非单独基准。基准验证必须优先于修复评估。研究发布重新验证的版本固定基准，为量子程序修复研究提供更可靠的评估基础。

Abstract: In quantum programs, Bugs4Q is a widely used benchmark containing real quantum defects. However, its evaluation assumes that benchmark labels remain valid and that generated fixes execute in the target environment. We evaluate two Bugs4Q versions containing 67 unique real Qiskit defects, adding executable tests where missing, and re-run all entries across six pinned Qiskit releases (0.25.0, 0.45.0, 1.0.0, 1.1.1, 2.0.0, and 2.3.1). We find that quantum benchmarks can suffer from silent label inversion: entries become invalid without errors when reference fixes stop executing or buggy programs no longer reproduce failures. Thus, correctness depends on the (benchmark, version) pair rather than the benchmark alone. We evaluate four LLMs (GPT-4o-mini, GPT-5o-mini, GPT-5.4, and GPT-5.4-mini), generating up to 10 repair candidates per defect and testing them across all versions. GPT-5.4 achieves the highest pass@10 (48.8%), followed by GPT-5.4-mini (47.3%), GPT-5o-mini (30.3%), and GPT-4o-mini (22.6%). All models perform best on Qiskit 0.45.0 and decline after the Qiskit 1.0 transition. Many failures arise from deprecated or incompatible APIs rather than incorrect repairs, and 64\% of successful repairs occur on entries invalid under the target version. We release a re-validated, version-pinned Bugs4Q benchmark and show that benchmark validation must precede repair evaluation.

Main category: cs.SE

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出TypeUp方法，基于LLM引导模型利用已有知识和逻辑推理能力，从相似代码变更中学习，自动根据旧类型注解和代码变更生成新的类型注解。

Abstract: Type annotations are more and more popular in Python projects to avoid type errors caused by Python's dynamic typing feature. In this work, we argue that obsolete type annotations can be reduced and even avoided by automatically updating type annotations alongside code changes. We refer to this task as "Just-In-Time (JIT) type annotation updating". To solve this task, we propose a novel LLM-based approach named TypeUp (Type Annotation Updator) to automate this task. TypeUp can automatically generate new type annotations based on the old type annotations and corresponding code changes. Specifically, TypeUp guides LLM to perform type annotation updates by eliciting its knowledge and logical reasoning power and learning from similar code changes. The evaluation results show that TypeUp outperforms state-of-the-art type infer approach (i.e., TypeGen) by 41.9% on our task. Moreover, we conducted an in-the-wild evaluation with real-world software projects, 20 out of 25 type annotation updates generated by our approach have already been confirmed by developers, showing our approach's practical value in real-world environments.

### [38] [Agentic Proof and Property-Based Testing via Property-Templates in Data-Intensive Computing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09072)
*Seongmin Lee,Yaoxuan Wu,Miryung Kim*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出基于属性模板的双轨验证框架，在Lean 4定理证明器中进行形式化验证，同时生成可执行的PySpark属性测试。模板将证明成功率提升最多2.6倍，幻觉减少59%，并将属性测试的意图错配从22降至1，成本降低最多5.7倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI生成代码的成本降低，软件工程的新瓶颈转向意图指定与验证。传统模糊测试不足以应对"耐久性危机"，需要将形式化证明与系统化属性测试相结合，但大规模验证面临属性验证和防止AI幻觉两个子问题。

Method: 提出属性模板（property templates）——带有洞的抽象参数化形式，涵盖数据分区、计算分解和数据流计算等原则（如聚合分解）。设计双轨代理验证框架：一条轨道在Lean 4中形式化验证模板的正确性，另一条将PBT模板实例化为可执行PySpark测试。

Result: 模板使证明成功率平均提升1.6倍（最高2.6倍），证明幻觉减少59%；PBT合成中意图错配从22降至1，合成成本平均降低3.8倍（最高5.7倍）；代码覆盖率超过现有Spark模糊测试工具，接近无引导的LLM-based PBT；双轨对比能发现形式模型与实现之间的差距。

Conclusion: 属性模板能同时解决形式化验证和属性测试中的核心问题，证明与PBT双轨互补可有效识别模型与实现之间的偏差，为AI驱动编程的可靠性保障提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: As the cost of code generation becomes cheaper with AI, the new bottleneck in software engineering has shifted to intent specification and validation. Overcoming this durability crisis of AI-driven coding requires more than traditional fuzzing: each candidate property must be proven correct over a model and shown to hold on the real implementation, making formal proof and systematic property-based testing (PBT) complementary. However, validating properties this way at scale requires solving two subproblems: verifying candidate properties and operationalizing PBT without AI hallucination. We hypothesize that recurring property patterns, cast as property templates--abstract, parameterized forms with holes--address both at once.
  This paper investigates recurring property patterns in Apache Spark. In data-intensive scalable computing systems, correctness properties arise from the principles of data partition, computation decomposition, and dataflow computation. For instance, aggregation decomposition relates a global function executed on the entire dataset to a local function followed by a recombiner. We design an agentic, dual-track validation framework that uses property templates to formally verify correctness in the Lean 4 theorem prover and instantiate PBT templates as executable PySpark tests. Our evaluation shows that property templates increase agentic proof engineering success by up to 2.6x (1.6x on average) and reduce proof hallucinations by 59%. Template-guided PBT synthesis reduces intent misalignments from 22 to 1 and cuts synthesis cost by up to 5.7x (3.8x on average). Template-guided synthesis further exceeds a state-of-the-art Spark fuzzer and approaches unguided LLM-based PBT on code coverage. Finally, comparing the two tracks is informative: when a proof succeeds yet a PBT finds a counterexample, the mismatch identifies a gap between the formal model and implementation.

Abstract: Recently, the emergence of Large Language Models (LLMs) has spurred a surge of research into automated unit test generation, yielding impressive performance and reducing manual effort. However, existing LLM-based approaches still suffer from two major limitations: (1) they follow rigid, procedural workflows that underutilize the autonomous reasoning potential of LLMs, making it difficult to dynamically adapt testing strategies based on real-time feedback; and (2) they rely on rule-based context extraction that is not tailored to test generation, failing to capture fine-grained code dependencies and test-specific knowledge required for deriving test requirements. In this paper, we propose TestAgent, an LLM-based test generation approach that addresses the above limitations by emulating human testing practices via a multi-agent collaboration mechanism. Particularly, TestAgent designs three specialized agents, namely a requirement planner, a test generator, and a test reviewer, to simulate how developers understand, construct, and validate unit tests. To unleash the autonomous capabilities of LLMs, we equip TestAgent with a set of tool APIs that can be invoked dynamically in an on-demand and adaptive manner. To further support repository-level reasoning, TestAgent constructs a test-specialized knowledge graph via static analysis, which captures code entities and their dependencies across the project and persistently stores testing artifacts (e.g., test reports and failure analyses) produced during generation. Experimental results show that TestAgent achieves 97.46% execution rate, 92.34% line coverage, 90.24% branch coverage, and 83.69% mutation score on six Java projects, outperforming LLM-based baselines across all metrics and achieving substantially higher mutation scores than search-based tools.
