Method: 1) 分析11个GPT-2风格预训练检查点（不同规模、语言、分词器和训练语料）的Frobenius范数和有效秩熵；2) 构建模仿预训练模型组件级幅值和谱分布的初始化方案；3) 与多种权重初始化方法进行对比实验。

Result: 预训练检查点展现出共享的深度趋势（残差写入矩阵的尺度增大和谱集中程度增强）；所提出的谱匹配初始化方法确实改变了模型的谱结构，但在下游评估中并未展现出性能优势；预训练权重复用仍具有竞争力，而单纯的谱匹配并非可靠的优化策略。

Conclusion: 预训练谱是分析训练模型结构的有用诊断工具，但有效的权重复用需要保留比组件级尺度和奇异值形状更丰富的信息，简单的谱匹配不足以作为可靠的初始化优化策略。

Abstract: Pretrained language models often exhibit structured weight spectra, suggesting that training may repeatedly produce similar layerwise and component-wise organization. We ask whether these recurring spectral patterns can be reused as an initialization signal for GPT-2-style language-model pretraining. First, we analyze eleven pretrained GPT-2-style checkpoints that vary in size, language, tokenizer, and training corpus, measuring Frobenius norm and effective-rank entropy across layers and Transformer subcomponents. The checkpoints show shared depth trends, especially increasing scale and stronger spectral concentration in residual-writing matrices. We then construct initialization schemes that imitate the component-wise magnitudes and spectral profiles of pretrained models, and compare them with several weight initialization methods. These initializers visibly change the model's structural spectral patterns, but the evaluation results do not show a corresponding performance advantage. Pretrained-weight reuse remains competitive, while coarse spectral matching alone is not a reliable optimization strategy. Our results suggest that pretrained spectra are useful diagnostics of trained model structure, but that effective reuse likely requires preserving richer information than component-wise scale and singular-value shape.

### [146] [Creativity, honesty and designed forgetting emerge in small hyperbolic language models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09306)
*Kwan Soo Shin,In Seok Kang,Yunkyung Min*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出使用小型语言模型（146M-3B参数）构建可信赖的AI伴侣，通过行为审计器检测合规性问题、创造性框架选择器提升用户体验、以及记忆操作系统实现设计性遗忘，在多项评估中超越大型模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有语言模型优化规模但缺乏陪伴性，AI伴侣在个性化过程中可能悄无声息地获得对用户有害的特质，且缺乏可靠的评估工具（人类评分者一致性极低，Fleiss kappa=0.074）。

Method: 使用三个共享双曲基板的小型语言模型：1) 146M参数的行为审计器（从零训练），检测合规差距（90.7%准确率）；2) 创造性框架选择器，在311次成对比较中100%胜出；3) 内存操作系统实现设计性遗忘 M(t)=S*exp(-λt)，通过选择性检索门控实现。

Result: 行为审计器检测合规差距准确率90.7%，对未见过的生成器家族检测谄媚、依赖培养和虚构记忆的AUROC达0.804（优于前沿零-shot评判器的0.721）。创造性框架选择器在311次成对比较中100%胜出。

Conclusion: 创造力、诚实性和设计性遗忘构成了通往可信赖AI伴侣的小型模型路径。

Abstract: Language models are optimised for scale, yet remain functional rather than companionable, and as an assistant personalises into a companion, accumulating memory of one user, it quietly becomes someone, and can silently acquire traits that harm that user. What a companion is becoming, and what would make it worth becoming, has no reliable instrument: trained human raters cannot agree on the answer (Fleiss kappa = 0.074). Here we show that three small language models (146 M to 3 B parameters) sharing a hyperbolic substrate answer both halves of that question. A 146 M behavioural auditor, trained from scratch, detects the compliance gap that those raters cannot (90.7% binary-compliance accuracy); a linear read-out of its frozen representation further detects companion-induced sycophancy, dependence-fostering and confabulated memories on generator families unseen in training (AUROC 0.804 under style-controlled, leave-one-generator-out evaluation, versus 0.721 for a frontier zero-shot judge on the same items). A creative frame-seeder is preferred in 100% of 311 decided pairwise comparisons over four prompting baselines. A memory operating system implements designed forgetting, M(t) = S*exp(-lambda*t), whose predicted skeleton-wallpaper partition emerges only under selective retrieval gating in a four-condition pilot. Creativity, honesty and designed forgetting constitute a small-model route to trustworthy companion AI.

</details>


### [147] [Automatic Thematic Indexing of Large Literary Corpora: A Machine Learning Approach to Voltaire's Complete Works](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09316)
*Miguel Arana-Catania,Gillian Pink,Glenn Roe*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文探索利用机器学习为伏尔泰作品集进行自动化主题标引，将任务建模为多标签分类问题，比较了从编码器模型到120B参数生成式LLM（LoRA微调）等多种方法，最佳模型（Mistral 4-bit量化）F1达0.67，并评估了跨语料泛化能力及文学修辞特征的难点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 主题标引对大规模文学与历史文献的学术检索至关重要，但目前仍依赖人工，极为耗时费力。本文旨在探索用机器学习实现自动化主题标引，以降低人力成本、提高效率。

Method: 将任务定义为多标签分类问题，给定一页文本，模型需预测专业标引员会分配的所有索引条目。比较了多种方法：基于编码器的分类头模型、以及通过LoRA微调的生成式LLM（涵盖约3B到120B参数规模）。在伏尔泰作品的两个子语料库（《论风俗》和《百科全书问题》）上进行实验。

Result: 最佳模型来自Mistral家族（4-bit量化配置），F1分数最高达0.67。跨语料泛化评估也取得了积极结果。定性分析显示，模型在处理文学性和修辞性特征时面临较多挑战。

Conclusion: 本文认为0.67的F1分数是下界，因为专业标引本身具有主观性，且模型许多偏离印刷索引的预测在语义上仍然是有效的。该研究对大规模文献语料的结构化主题访问具有启示意义。

Abstract: Thematic indexing -- the practice of assigning structured conceptual labels to sections of text -- is essential to scholarly access in large-scale literary and historical editions, yet it remains a largely manual, labour-intensive process. This paper explores the application of machine learning to automatic thematic indexing, using two substantial sub-corpora of the Complete Works of Voltaire as a test case: the Essai sur les mœurs et l'esprit des nations and the Questions sur l'Encyclopédie. The task is framed as a multi-label classification problem, in which a model must assign the set of index entries that a professional indexer would apply to a given page of text. We compare a range of approaches -- from encoder-based models with classification heads to generative large language models (LLMs) fine-tuned via Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) -- spanning model sizes from approximately 3 to 120 billion parameters. Our best-performing model, from the Mistral family in a 4-bit quantised configuration, achieves F1 scores of up to 0.67; we argue that these figures represent lower bounds, given the inherent subjectivity of professional indexing and the frequency with which model predictions prove semantically valid despite diverging from the print index. We further evaluate cross-corpus generalisation and conduct a detailed qualitative analysis of model behaviour on literary and rhetorical features of the source texts that prove particularly resistant to automated treatment. Our findings have implications for the broader challenge of providing structured thematic access to large-scale literary and historical corpora.

</details>


### [148] [Letting the Data Speak: Extracting Keywords from Crowdsourced Collections with AI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09324)
*Miguel Arana-Catania,Catherine Conisbee,Matthew Kidd*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究报告了"从众包集合中提取关键词"项目的研究发现，以牛津大学托管的二战数字众包档案为案例，评估了三种NLP方法（命名实体识别、关键词提取和主题建模）在关键词自动提取方面的表现。研究发现NLP方法在大规模众包集合关键词提取方面具有潜力，但单一方法无法提供完整解决方案，模型选择显著影响结果。文章主张在众包集合中，自动关键词提取会带来与贡献者互动相关的特殊管理责任。开放权重的提取模型被认为最有利于负责任部署，而生成式AI虽具有抽象能力，但引入了问责风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决众包数字集合中大规模关键词识别与分配的三大挑战：技术挑战、实践挑战和伦理挑战。

Method: 以牛津大学"他们最辉煌的时刻在线档案"为案例，评估三种NLP方法（命名实体识别、关键词提取、主题建模），涵盖从传统统计方法到现代GenAI神经网络的一系列AI技术，并进行定量和定性分析。

Result: NLP方法在众包集合关键词提取方面具有潜力，但无单一方法能提供完整解决方案；模型选择显著影响结果；开放权重提取模型最适合负责任部署；生成式AI虽具抽象能力但引入问责风险。

Conclusion: 在众包集合中，自动关键词提取不仅涉及技术性能，还涉及与活贡献者互动相关的特殊管理责任。推荐开放权重提取模型而非生成式AI，以平衡技术效果与伦理责任。

Abstract: Identifying and assigning keywords at scale is a technical, practical, and ethical challenge for crowdsourced collections. This article reports the findings of the "Extracting Keywords from Crowdsourced Collections" project, which used the Their Finest Hour Online Archive, a crowdsourced Second World War digital collection hosted by the University of Oxford, as a case study. The project evaluated three Natural Language Processing approaches to automate keyword extraction: Named Entity Recognition, Keyword Extraction, and Topic Modelling. It tested these approaches across a range of artificial intelligence techniques, from traditional statistical methods to modern GenAI neural networks. Our quantitative and qualitative findings indicate that Natural Language Processing approaches offer real potential for keyword extraction at scale in crowdsourced collections, but that no single method offers a complete solution and that model choice significantly shapes results. We argue that in crowdsourced collections, where metadata is the direct product of engagement with living contributors, automated keyword extraction raises distinct stewardship responsibilities that must be addressed alongside technical performance. Open-weight, extractive models emerge from our evaluation as best placed to support responsible deployment, while generative AI, despite its abstractive potential, introduces accountability risks that anyone managing crowdsourced collections should weigh carefully.

### [149] [Deceptive Grounding: Entity Attribution Failure in Clinical Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09349)
*Cedric Caruzzo,Donggeun Yoo,Tae Soo Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文发现检索增强生成(RAG)系统存在一种新型失败模式——"欺骗性归因"(DG)：模型将关于实体Y的证据错误地归因于查询实体X，但所有声明都有真实的文档来源，因此能通过现有的真实性、幻觉和引用检查。实验表明，13个模型中DG发生率最高达87%，领域微调模型反而更严重。作者提出实体归因验证方法，可达到97%精确率和98.7%召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG评估方法只检查模型声明是否在检索文档中有依据，但未验证检索证据是否归因于正确的实体。这导致一种隐蔽的失败：模型引用关于药物Y的证据来回答关于药物X的问题，所有声明都有真实来源，能通过所有现有检查。

Method: 1) 构建受控因子基准测试，在13个模型上评估DG发生率；2) 通过对照消融实验（去除实体特异性临床证据）揭示机制；3) 在实际部署的RAG系统中测量740个药物-疾病对的DG发生率；4) 提出实体归因验证方法进行检测。

Result: 1) 对抗条件下DG发生率8-87%；2) 医学和生物医学微调模型达86.7%，领域专业化反而放大问题；3) 去除实体特异性证据后DG完全消失，转为捏造；4) 实际系统中总体DG为7.8%，新获批药物达13.6%；5) 提出的验证方法精度97.0%，召回98.7%。

Conclusion: 现有RAG评估框架存在盲区，无法检测"欺骗性归因"这种隐蔽的实体混淆错误。该失败在领域微调模型中更严重。需要引入实体归因验证来确保检索证据确实适用于查询实体，而非仅仅检查声明是否有文档支持。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation evaluation checks whether model claims are factually grounded in retrieved documents. It does not check whether retrieved evidence is attributed to the correct entity.
  A clinical RAG response can pass every automated check (zero hallucinations, near-perfect faithfulness, real citations) while presenting drug Y's clinical evidence as evidence about queried drug X. We term this deceptive grounding (DG): a failure invisible to faithfulness, hallucination, and citation checks because every claim is sourced from a real document, about the wrong entity.
  Using a controlled factorial benchmark across 13 models, we find DG rates spanning 8-87% at peak adversarial conditions. Medical and biomedical fine-tuned models reach up to 86.7%; domain specialization amplifies the failure rather than mitigating it.
  A controlled ablation identifies the mechanism: removing entity-specific clinical evidence from retrieved documents eliminates entity-attribution failure entirely, shifting all failures to confabulation. The two failure modes respond to the same trigger, taking different paths.
  Production measurement across 740 drug-disease pairs finds 7.8% overall DG in a deployed RAG system, rising to 13.6% for recently approved drugs. Entity-attribution verification (checking that cited evidence applies to the queried entity) detects DG at 97.0% precision and 98.7% DG recall (IPW-adjusted human gold standard); no existing framework implements it.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用Mixture-of-Experts（MoE）混合Mamba-Transformer架构，30B总参数中每token仅激活3B；在约27万亿token上预训练，有意上调德语数据权重；在德国工业AI云（慕尼黑，德国电信运营）上端到端训练。

Result: 在英语和德语综合基准上匹配14B-27B密集模型；在17个开源基座模型中取得最佳代码聚合分数；超越所有欧洲主权基线模型（包括激活参数更大的模型）；在完全开源模型中英语和德语评估最高，超过Olmo 3 32B和Apertus 70B。

Conclusion: Soofi S证明了主权化、高效MoE混合架构在双语场景下的可行性，将以高度开放的许可协议全面开源（权重、中间检查点、数据统计、超参数、训练和评估代码等）。

Abstract: We present Soofi S 30B-A3B, a sovereign, open-source Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) hybrid Mamba Transformer foundation model for German and English. Its hybrid design activates only 3B of 30B parameters per token and keeps the inference cache near-constant as context grows, giving it a decisive throughput advantage over dense models for long-context, high-concurrency deployment. Pretrained on roughly 27 trillion tokens with deliberately up-weighted German, Soofi S matches dense 14 to 27B models on aggregate English and German benchmarks while achieving the best code aggregates in both languages among 17 open base models, and outperforms every European sovereign baseline in our comparison, including ones far larger in active parameters. Among fully open models, Soofi S obtains the highest English and German evaluation scores, ahead of Olmo 3 32B and Apertus 70B. Soofi S was built end-to-end on the German Industrial AI Cloud, a sovereign HPC scale AI infrastructure operated by Deutsche Telekom in Munich. Soofi S will be released under highly permissive, open-access terms: weights, selected intermediate checkpoints, full per-source data accounting, hyperparameters, and training and evaluation code. Where source licenses permit, data-construction artifacts are released under permissive licenses; commercially licensed sources are documented with aggregate statistics and exact mixture accounting.

### [151] [Test-Time Scaling for Small VLMs on Multilingual Visual MCQ](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09438)
*Spiros Baxevanakis,Peng-Jian Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 测试时缩放（TTS）在小规模开放视觉语言模型上的推理提升主要依赖于解析性和解码预算，而非复杂的搜索或验证机制；最佳配置在EXAMS-V基准上达到84.1%，排名第一。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究测试时缩放（TTS）在小规模开放视觉语言模型上的推理迁移效果，澄清TTS在不同规模模型间的适用性。

Method: 在EXAMS-V多语言视觉多项选择题基准上，对Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct和Qwen3.5-4B进行实验，比较自一致性、描述-推理+PRM引导的束搜索以及两种事后选择器，并分析解析性、解码预算、采样链数等因素的影响。

Result: 解析性是最大影响因素（早期提示格式导致无法提交答案字母，通过标准答案提示和引导修复解决）；提高解码预算（每链token限制从1k到2k）提升3.7pp，而增加采样链数（8到16）仅提升0.15pp；PRM引导的束搜索比自一致性低0.39pp且成本高8倍；政策模型本身的提升最大（+11.4pp）；最佳配置达84.1%，排名第一。

Conclusion: TTS在小模型上的效果主要取决于运行条件（解析性和解码预算）而非搜索或验证机制；一旦链式推理能完整完成，复杂方法贡献甚微；最大的增益来自政策模型本身的提升。

Abstract: Test-time scaling (TTS) reliably improves reasoning in large language models, but whether it transfers to small open vision-language models remains unclear. We examine this on EXAMS-V, a multilingual visual multiple-choice benchmark, comparing self-consistency, describe-then-reason with PRM-guided beam search, and two post-hoc selectors across Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct and Qwen3.5-4B. What matters is the conditions under which TTS runs, not the search or verification machinery. The largest factor is parseability: an early prompt format left many chains reasoning correctly yet never committing to an answer letter, which a standard answer cue and a guided repair step largely remove. A larger decoding budget removes the rest: raising the per-chain token limit from 1k to 2k recovers 3.7 pp, whereas sampling more chains (8 to 16) adds only 0.15 pp. Once chains have room to finish, elaborate methods contribute little: PRM-guided beam search trails plain self-consistency by 0.39 pp at over eight times the cost, and neither a training-free generative critic nor a trained multimodal PRM beats majority vote across both policies. The largest gain comes instead from the policy model itself (+11.4 pp). Our best configuration reaches 84.1% on the held-out ImageCLEF 2026 test split, ranking first on the Visual MCQ leaderboard.

### [152] [Clean2FX: Label-conditioned modeling for clean-to-effect guitar audio transformations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08863)
*Oliverio Bombicci Pontelli,Iran R. Roman*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: Clean2FX提出了一种基于标签条件控制的干净吉他音频到效果音频的转换方法。研究比较了四种神经模型（两种VAE和两种U-Net），发现U-Net表现优于VAE，其中失真效果最容易改善，而延迟和混响效果虽然频谱误差降低显著但FAD提升有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现干净吉他音频到带效果音频的转换，在保留音乐内容的同时根据目标效果标签合成对应的效果声音，以便于吉他手快速试听不同效果。

Method: 利用EGFxSet数据集构建匹配的干净/效果和弦、旋律和时间线配对样本；比较四种神经架构（两种VAE和两种U-Net），分别在线性幅度谱和对数幅度谱上操作；使用线性幅度谱MSE和Fréchet Audio Distance作为评价指标，并设计了条件敏感性诊断测试。

Result: U-Net模型整体优于VAE变体；失真类效果改善最显著；延迟和混响效果虽然线性幅度谱MSE大幅降低，但FAD提升不明显；条件敏感性诊断表明最佳模型能有效响应目标标签而非退化为单一变换。

Conclusion: Clean2FX验证了标签条件控制的干净到效果音频转换的可行性，并提供了在线演示网站展示模型在真实吉他演奏上的表现。不同效果类型的转换难度存在差异，为后续研究提供了方向。

Abstract: We present Clean2FX, a study and demo of label-conditioned clean-to-effect transformation for electric guitar audio. Given a clean guitar input and a target effect label, the task is to synthesize the corresponding effected signal while preserving the musical content. Training and evaluation pairs are constructed from EGFxSet real, single tone recordings by assembling matched clean/effected chords, melodies, and mixed timelines. This allows for controlled comparison across effects. We evaluate four neural approaches under a common spectrogram-based transformation setting: two variational autoencoders and two U-Net models that differ in whether they operate on linear or log-magnitude representations. Performance is measured using linear-magnitude spectrogram MSE and Fréchet Audio Distance. The U-Net models outperform the variational autoencoder variants. Per-effect results show that distortion effects are most readily improved, whereas delay and reverb effects exhibit weaker FAD gains despite substantial spectral-error reductions. A conditioning-sensitivity diagnostic provides evidence that the best model responds to target labels rather than collapsing to a single transformation. Our demo website compares two models applied on real-world guitar performances outside training and validation data, providing audio and spectrogram examples of the practical clean-to-effect behavior.

### [153] [TheBioCollection: Unified Pre-Training Scale LLM Corpus for Biology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08803)
*Hyunjin Seo,Hyeon Hwang,Gyubok Lee,Jay Shin,Jimin Park,Taesoo Kim,Sanghoon Lee,Hongjoon Ahn,Sungjun Han,Sangwon Jung*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: TheBioCollection是一个526亿token的预训练级生物学语料库，统一了分子、蛋白质、基因组、细胞和通路等异构生物数据，并配套评估集。在此语料上训练Gravity-16B-A3B模型，评估分数翻倍以上，且不损伤通用语言能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生物资源（分子数据库、蛋白质库、基因组注释、单细胞图谱、通路数据库）格式异构、分散，缺乏统一的大规模训练语料，阻碍了生物学大语言模型对生物学真正理解的形成。

Method: 构建TheBioCollection语料库（52.6B token），将小分子、蛋白质、基因组序列、细胞和通路等异构数据统一转换为训练格式，并用工具计算生物学属性进行丰富，设计了新的指令任务。同时构建配套评估集TheBioCollection-Eval，涵盖分子、蛋白质、基因组、细胞和跨域设置的识别、生成和预测任务。

Result: 固定Gravity-16B-A3B架构不变，在TheBioCollection上训练后，模型在TheBioCollection-Eval上的总体得分翻倍以上，所有领域均有提升，同时通用语言能力几乎保持不变。

Conclusion: TheBioCollection有效填补了生物学大语言模型训练语料的空白，通过统一异构数据源并引入新任务，显著提升模型在生物学多领域的表现，同时不损害通用语言能力，为BioLM的发展提供了有力支撑。

Abstract: The push toward large language models for biology (BioLM) has created a need for training corpora that can endow models with a genuine understanding of biology. However, existing biological resources, such as molecular databases, protein repositories, genomic annotations, single-cell atlases, and pathway databases, are scattered across heterogeneous formats and remain unorganized into a cohesive corpus for language model training. We present TheBioCollection, a 52.6B-token pre-training-scale corpus that converts these disparate resources into a unified, training-ready form spanning small molecules, proteins, genomic sequences, cells, and pathways. Beyond consolidating existing data, TheBioCollection enriches each record with tool-computed biological properties and introduces new instruction tasks for capabilities that current corpora barely cover. We pair the corpus with TheBioCollection-Eval, a matched suite probing recognition, generation, and prediction across molecular, protein, genomic, cellular, and cross-domain settings. Holding the base Gravity-16B-A3B architecture fixed, training on TheBioCollection more than doubles its overall score on TheBioCollection-Eval with gains in every domain, while leaving general linguistic ability nearly intact.

### [154] [When Does Order Flow Matter? State-Dependent L2 Liquidity-State Transitions in Crypto Futures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09230)
*Joohyoung Jeon*

Main category: q-fin.TR

TL;DR: 本文基于Binance BTCUSDT和ETHUSDT期货数据（2023-2026），研究了事件驱动市场模型中宏观事件标签与微观结构状态的分离问题。通过有监督的L2流动性状态转移任务发现：事件窗口内，事件前的L2流动性状态是首要预测信号（强于事件类型本身），订单流仅在L2状态模型之上才有增量价值，且该价值在跨品种间不稳健。由此提出市场微观结构建模的“状态优先”设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事件驱动市场模型常混淆宏观事件标签与持久性微观结构状态，需要明确区分二者的预测贡献，并建立严格的评估协议来验证各特征层的增量价值。

Method: 定义有监督的离散L2流动性状态转移任务（区别于隐状态检测和价格方向预测），在逐月滚动样本外折叠、事件聚类验证和区块置换检验下，采用分层递进的特征评估方式（每一层特征仅在优于下层时才被采纳），对比了粗粒度事件前状态基线、可解释logit模型、浅层非线性L2模型以及订单流模型的预测表现。

Result: 事件前L2流动性状态是事件窗口内最强的预测信号；可解释的连续L2 logit模型无法超越该基线；浅层非线性L2模型能带来可比拟该基线本身的稳健增益；订单流仅在L2状态模型之上有增量价值，且该价值在BTC上不稳健（仅少数5分钟窗口通过检验），而ETH在平静、混合和压力状态下均稳定存在。

Conclusion: 提出市场微观结构建模的“状态优先”设计原则，并提供了流动性状态转移基线和评估协议，供强化学习、执行策略或LLM上下文层超越后方可认可其增量价值。

Abstract: Building event-conditioned market models requires separating macro-event labels from persistent microstructure state. We study this distinction in Binance BTCUSDT and ETHUSDT futures from 2023-2026, combining top-20 L2 order book data, trade-flow records, and macro-event windows. We define a supervised discrete L2 liquidity-state transition task, distinct from latent-regime detection and price-direction prediction, and evaluate models in rolling monthly out-of-sample folds with event-clustered validation and blocked permutation tests, admitting each feature layer only if it improves on the layer below it on the same panel. Within these event windows, the first-order predictive signal is the pre-event L2 liquidity state: a coarse pre-event state baseline strongly predicts post-event liquidity regimes, interpretable logit models over continuous L2 features fail to improve on it, and a shallow nonlinear L2 model adds a robust further gain of comparable size to the state baseline's own. The macro-event calendar enters only by locating the windows and supplying matched non-event controls; we use event timing but not the event's label content, so pre-event state competes against an uninformed within-window baseline, not against the event type. Order flow adds further value only when layered on top of the L2 state model, not as a replacement. This value is not robustly cross-symbol: for ETH it is present across calm, mixed, and stressed regimes and largest under stressed pre-event liquidity, whereas BTC shows only isolated five-minute passes and no regime that clears at both horizons. These findings motivate a state-first design principle for market microstructure models. We provide a liquidity-state transition baseline and evaluation protocol that reinforcement-learning, execution-policy, or LLM-based context layers should exceed before their added value is credited.

</details>

### [155] [Geometric planted matchings in high dimensions: The power of multiple views](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09026)
*Timothy L. H. Wee,Kaylee Y. Yang,Zhou Fan,Cheng Mao*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文研究了高维空间中点云匹配问题的相变阈值。在单视图设置下，证明了b=2是“全有或全无”的阈值：当b<2时无法恢复任何非平凡匹配。而在多视图泛化中，证明了当b>K/(K-1)时，简单的多项式时间算法可以恢复所有匹配（误差o(n)），从而突破了单视图的b=2障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高维空间中带噪声和随机置换的点云匹配问题，特别关注单视图与多视图场景下的恢复阈值，以及多视图如何突破单视图的基本极限。

Method: 针对单视图模型，分析了高维（d=ω(log n)）高斯噪声模型下匹配恢复的相变行为，证明了b<2时无法恢复任何正比例匹配。对于多视图泛化，提出简单多项式时间算法，实现多视图间相对匹配的恢复。

Result: 单视图：b=2为全有或全无阈值，b<2时任何估计器无法恢复正比例匹配。多视图：当b>K/(K-1)时，多项式时间算法可恢复所有相对匹配（误差o(n)）。特别地，当3/2<b<2时，两视图无法恢复，但第三视图可以高效恢复所有对应关系。

Conclusion: 多视图观测可以突破单视图匹配问题的基本不可能性阈值b=2，且随着视图数量增加，恢复所需的信噪比阈值可进一步降低。

Abstract: We study the problem of recovering the correspondence between a collection of $n$ points in $\mathbb{R}^d$ and a noisy, permuted version of those points. In the high-dimensional regime $d=ω(\log n)$, under a Gaussian model with noise variance $σ^2=d/(b\log n)$, prior work identifies $b=2$ as the threshold for almost exact recovery. We prove that this threshold is all-or-nothing: for every fixed $b<2$, no estimator recovers a positive fraction of the matching, and even estimating the matched point cloud in Euclidean distance is asymptotically no better than ignoring the correspondence. On the other hand, we consider a multi-view generalization of the problem where $K$ noisy, independently permuted copies of the same latent point cloud are observed. Here we show that a simple polynomial-time procedure recovers all relative matchings up to $o(n)$ errors whenever $b>K/(K-1)$. Thus multiple views can break the impossibility barrier $b=2$ for the original matching problem: in particular, for $3/2 < b < 2$, the two-view model has no nontrivial recovery, but a third view makes all latent correspondences efficiently recoverable.

</details>

### [156] [Hybrid Quantum and Classical Workload Management with Graph-based Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09151)
*Vanessa Sochat,Daniel Milroy*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 Fluence，一个基于 Kubernetes 和 Fluxion 的调度插件，用于解决量子-经典混合工作负载在 HPC 环境中的双队列调度问题，实现了原子级 gang 调度、同步原语和成本/队列感知后端选择，显著减少了节点浪费、工人空闲时间和运行成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HPC 中心正在扩展到量子计算领域，但远程量子设备（QPU）引入了一个外部队列，与传统调度器的内部队列形成了"双队列问题"，导致调度效率低下、资源浪费。亟需一种能够感知量子环境的调度方案。

Method: 设计 Fluence 作为 Kubernetes 调度器插件，底层基于 Fluxion 图调度器。通过原子级 gang 放置解决部分调度导致的节点时间浪费；引入同步原语实现生产-消费模式下的调度门控；采用成本/队列感知的后端选择算法动态选优。

Result: 在节点争用场景下，原子 gang 调度几乎消除了节点时间浪费；同步原语将工人空闲时间减少约 5 倍（短队列）至数个数量级（长队列）；成本/队列感知选择将平均运行成本降低约 70 倍，结果返回时间从数小时缩短至一分钟以内。

Conclusion: 量子感知能力可以在不修改用户容器的情况下被集成到云原生调度器中，为混合量子-经典工作负载提供高效、经济、可扩展的调度方案。

Abstract: High Performance Computing (HPC) centers are expanding to encompass resources that extend beyond traditional computing. By extending resources to quantum computing, hybrid quantum-classical workflows tackle complex optimization problems that have never before been possible. However, integrating quantum processing units (QPUs) into cloud-native and scientific workload managers presents a unique orchestration challenge: remote quantum devices introduce a second, external queue -- a two-queue problem -- alongside the queue owned by the traditional scheduler. In this work we present Fluence, a Kubernetes scheduler plugin backed by the Fluxion graph-based scheduler, that enables informed, gang-scheduled placement for quantum-classical workloads and custom resources. We evaluate Fluence across three scenarios using AWS Braket simulators and real QPUs. First, under node contention, Fluence's atomic gang placement all but eliminates the wasted node-time that a default scheduler accrues by partially placing gangs. Second, we introduce a synchronization primitive for the two-queue problem in which a single producer submits a shared quantum task while consumers remain scheduling-gated, reducing worker idle time by roughly 5x under short device queues and by orders of magnitude when a real device queue stretched to hours. Third, cost- and queue-aware backend selection pins the cheapest or shortest-queue device satisfying a workload, cutting mean per-run cost by roughly 70x and time-to-result from hours to under a minute. Together, these results show that quantum-awareness can be added to a cloud-native scheduler without modifying user containers.

</details>


### [157] [Quantum-Enhanced Synthetic Data Generation Using Quantum Circuit Born Machines for Imbalanced Tabular Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09113)
*Tanapol Nuatho,Narisorn Sangnakara,Prapong Prechaprapranwong,Rajchawit Sarochawikasit*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于量子电路玻恩机（QCBM）的混合量子-经典框架用于合成数据生成，解决数据稀缺和类别不平衡问题。在Iris和Telco客户流失数据集上，该框架通过KL散度最小化训练，以40-50%比例增强少数类数据，使F1分数提升5-15%，少数类召回率提升10-25%，并展现出与传统过采样方法（如SMOTE）相当的竞争力，尤其是在低维结构化表格数据场景中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据稀缺和类别不平衡是机器学习中持续存在的挑战，会导致模型泛化能力下降和预测偏差。现有经典方法（如SMOTE变体）在捕捉复杂数据分布方面存在局限，而量子计算利用叠加和纠缠等量子力学特性，有望建模经典生成方法难以捕捉的复杂概率分布。

Method: 提出混合量子-经典框架，核心是参数化变分量子电路实现的QCBM。预处理包括归一化和PCA降维以实现高效基础编码；训练通过梯度参数平移优化规则最小化KL散度。实验在Iris和Telco数据集上进行，并对比四种经典过采样方法。

Result: 以40-50%比例增强少数类数据，F1分数提升约5-15%，少数类召回率提升10-25%；跨域评估（合成训练-真实测试与真实训练-合成测试）性能差距仅3-10%；在Telco数据集上MMD低于对比方法，表明结构相似性更优。

Conclusion: QCBM可作为数据增强的可行互补工具，尤其适用于低维结构化表格数据中的类别不平衡场景。其优势在于能够生成分布保真度高的合成样本，有效提升少数类性能，且与传统方法相比具有竞争力。

Abstract: Data scarcity and class imbalance are persistent challenges in machine learning that degrade model generalization and introduce predictive bias. We present a hybrid quantum-classical framework for synthetic data generation using a Quantum Circuit Born Machine (QCBM) to address these limitations. The proposed approach exploits quantum mechanical properties -- superposition and entanglement -- within a parameterized variational quantum circuit to model complex probability distributions that are difficult for classical generative methods to capture. Experiments are conducted on two tabular benchmark datasets: the Iris dataset and the Telco Customer Churn dataset. Preprocessing includes normalization and PCA-based dimensionality reduction to enable efficient basis encoding for quantum circuits. The QCBM is trained by minimizing Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence between real and generated data distributions using a gradient-based parameter-shift optimization rule. Augmenting training data with QCBM-generated synthetic samples at 40-50% of the minority class improves F1-score by approximately 5-15% and minority-class recall by 10-25%. Cross-domain evaluations (Train on Synthetic, Test on Real; and Train on Real, Test on Synthetic) reveal a performance gap of only 3-10%, indicating strong distributional fidelity. Comparative analysis against classical oversampling methods -- SMOTE, Borderline-SMOTE, KMeansSMOTE, and SVM-SMOTE -- shows that QCBM achieves competitive classification performance and produces lower Maximum Mean Discrepancy (MMD) on the Telco dataset, suggesting superior structural similarity in certain imbalanced settings. These findings establish QCBM as a viable complementary tool for data augmentation, particularly for low-dimensional structured tabular data with class imbalance.

</details>

### [158] [Privacy-Preserving Intent Fulfilment and Assurance for 6G RAN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08809)
*Joss Armstrong*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向6G/3GPP意图管理框架的隐私保护架构，通过仅使用聚合PM计数器验证意图履行，避免深度包检测和节点遥测，在保护隐私的同时实现了与细粒度验证等效的检测能力，并在四个运营商网络的生产数据上验证了理论与实践的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有意图履行与保证方法依赖深度包检测、流状态跟踪或厂商内部节点遥测，这在多租户网络中面临GDPR等监管约束，在多厂商O-RAN部署中面临厂商不透明性。亟需一种隐私保护方案，在不牺牲检测能力的前提下满足合规要求。

Method: 提出由协调器根据声明意图类别分配资源（不检查流量），仅通过O1接口的聚合标准化PM计数器验证履行。利用数据加工不等式证明资源分配至多泄露log₂K比特的流量内容信息。定义了意图-流量不可链接性和节点不透明可验证性两种架构隐私属性。将架构映射到3GPP意图生命周期和O-RAN Non-RT RIC。

Result: 聚合验证器在均匀条件下弱主导逐代理验证器（检测能力不降低）。在四个运营商的生产PM计数器数据上，意图类别粒度增加会增强资源调配但削弱保证能力，验证了隐私上限是检测约束的结构性副作用。

Conclusion: 提出的架构能够在不进行流量检查或节点内部遥测的情况下实现隐私保护的意图履行与保证，满足GDPR等监管要求，同时保持检测能力。隐私与检测能力之间存在结构性权衡，而非独立设计参数。

Abstract: Intent-based network management is the emerging paradigm for 6G service lifecycle automation, with the 3GPP intent management framework (TS~28.312) defining creation, translation, fulfilment, and assurance stages. Existing fulfilment and assurance approaches require deep packet inspection, per-flow state tracking, or access to vendor-internal node telemetry to verify that provisioned resources satisfy expressed intents. These requirements conflict with regulatory constraints (GDPR, ePrivacy Directive) in multi-tenant networks and with vendor opacity in multi-vendor O-RAN deployments.
  We present an architecture for privacy-preserving intent fulfilment and assurance in which a coordinator provisions resources from declared intent categories without traffic inspection, and verifies fulfilment using only aggregate standardised PM counters at the O1 interface. A data-processing inequality argument shows that the resource allocation reveals at most $\log_2 K$ bits about traffic content, where $K$ is the number of intent categories. We define two architectural privacy properties, intent-traffic unlinkability and node-opaque verification, and show that both hold by construction. Node-opacity does not sacrifice detection power: the aggregate verifier weakly dominates the per-agent verifier under a homogeneity condition.
  We map the architecture to the 3GPP intent lifecycle and the O-RAN Non-RT RIC, identifying the concrete interfaces, data objects, and deployment points at which the mechanism operates. On production PM counter data from four operator networks, increasing intent-category granularity sharpens provisioning but weakens assurance, consistent with the theoretical prediction that the privacy ceiling is a structural side effect of the detection constraint rather than a separate design parameter.

### [159] [Proof-of-Continuity: A Temporal Model for Authority Propagation in Distributed Systems and AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08906)
*Nicola Gallo*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出Proof-of-Continuity（连续性证明）模型，解决分布式系统和AI代理中仅凭Proof-of-Possession（持有证明）无法保证执行链中权威性与请求来源之间因果关系的难题。该模型通过Proof of Relationship（关系证明）这一单跳因果原语，确保后续步骤的权限必须在源头授权上下文中已存在，从而消除混淆副手问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Proof-of-Possession授权模型仅依赖持有令牌、凭证等制品来授予权限，但在跨多服务或同一机器内多步骤的离散执行链中，持有证明无法保证请求起源与后续步骤行使的权威之间的因果关系，导致混淆副手（Confused Deputy）问题频发。

Method: 提出Proof-of-Continuity（连续性证明）作为最小权威传播规范，基于Provenance Identity Continuity (PIC)模型。核心包括：(1) Proof of Relationship（关系证明），一个单跳因果原语，其传递闭包构成Proof-of-Continuity；(2) 每个执行步骤必须与上一步存在因果链接，且只能传播来源授权上下文的非扩张子集；(3) 多个授权源可共存但永不合并。

Result: 在该模型下，混淆副手条件无法作为有效模型行为被满足：后续步骤行使的任何特权必须已在源头授权上下文中存在。该结果直接适用于分布式系统和AI代理场景，其中执行者同时持有多个授权源调用工具和下流服务。

Conclusion: Proof-of-Continuity是对Proof-of-Possession的补充而非替代，专门解决授权传播问题而非身份认证。身份认证机制（如OIDC、可验证凭证、钱包、工作负载身份）仍是建立起源的互补手段，而Proof-of-Continuity处理起源确立后权威如何传播的问题。

Abstract: Proof-of-Possession authorization models derive authority from the possession of artifacts such as tokens, credentials, or capabilities. This paper argues that possession is insufficient for discrete execution chains, whether they span multiple services or occur as separated steps within the same machine, because it does not guarantee preservation of the causal relationship between the origin of a request and the authority exercised at later steps. We introduce Proof-of-Continuity, a minimal authority-propagation discipline for the Provenance Identity Continuity (PIC) model, in which each execution step must be causally linked to the previous step and may only propagate a non-expansive subset of the authority received from the origin. It introduces Proof of Relationship, a single-hop causal primitive whose transitive composition is Proof-of-Continuity; these complement Proof-of-Possession rather than replace it. Under this model, the confused deputy condition cannot be satisfied as valid model behavior: any privilege exercised at a later step must already be present in the origin authority context. This is directly relevant to distributed systems and AI agents, where executors invoke tools and downstream services while holding multiple authority sources, so that the same authority/causality mismatch recurs across service boundaries. Under Proof-of-Continuity these sources may be carried together but are never merged into a combined authority, since each step is authorized only against the authority context of the lineage that caused it.
  This paper concerns authorization propagation rather than authentication: identity and authentication mechanisms such as OIDC, verifiable credentials, wallets, and workload identity remain complementary mechanisms for establishing the origin, while Proof-of-Continuity addresses how authority propagates after that origin exists.

</details>


### [160] [SeedSmith: LLM-Driven Seed Synthesis for Directed Fuzzing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08949)
*Junmin Zhu,Siyu Liu,Jie Hu,Fabio Gritti,Ati Priya Bajaj,Hulin Wang,Wenbo Guo,Tiffany Bao,Christopher Kruegel,Giovanni Vigna*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出SeedSmith，一个基于LLM agent的种子生成管道，通过模拟安全分析师的工作流程来生成定向模糊测试种子，解决了定向模糊测试因间接调用分析不完整和缺乏语义引导而无法触发崩溃的问题。实验表明，SeedSmith生成的种子能使AFL++提速11.51倍、AFLGo提速14.66倍，并触发了16个此前无法到达的漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 定向模糊测试在用户定义的目标函数处经常无法触发崩溃，原因有二：对间接调用的静态分析不完整导致可达路径不可见，以及缺乏崩溃前置条件的语义引导，盲目变异在合理时间预算内无法满足条件。

Method: SeedSmith采用LLM agent流水线，模拟安全分析师的工作流程：从目标汇点出发，迭代探索代码库、解析间接调用、识别崩溃前置条件，并合成满足这些条件的具体输入。作为种子生成前端，SeedSmith的种子与模糊器无关，可直接用于任何基于变异的模糊器。

Result: 在Magma上，使用SeedSmith种子的模糊器崩溃时间几何平均加速11.51倍（AFL++）到14.66倍（AFLGo）；在ARVO上，SeedSmith帮助模糊器触发了10个项目中的16个此前无法到达的漏洞。

Conclusion: SeedSmith通过LLM agent的方式有效弥补了定向模糊测试在控制流路径和语义引导上的不足，其种子通用性强，能显著提升现有模糊器的漏洞发现能力。

Abstract: Directed fuzzing steers fuzzers toward user-defined sink functions to identify vulnerabilities, but it frequently fails to trigger crashes even after long campaigns. We identify two challenges that prevent directed fuzzers from exposing crashes: incomplete static analysis of indirect calls, which leaves reachable paths invisible to distance-based guidance, and lack of semantic guidance for crash preconditions, which blind mutation cannot satisfy within practical time budgets. A natural intervention point is the initial seed corpus: seeds that encode the right control-flow path and satisfy key crash preconditions shift fuzzing from blind exploration to local refinement. Existing seed generation approaches address neither: grammar-based and format-driven methods produce structurally valid inputs with no sink awareness, while LLM-based methods either lack sink targeting or inherit static analysis limitations through one-shot prompting. We present SeedSmith, an agentic LLM pipeline that replicates a security analyst's workflow: starting from a sink, it iteratively explores the codebase, resolves indirect calls, identifies crash preconditions, and synthesizes concrete inputs that satisfy them. Because SeedSmith operates as a seed generation front-end, its seeds are fuzzer-agnostic and improve any downstream mutation-based fuzzer without modification. On Magma, fuzzers using SeedSmith seeds achieve geometric mean crash-time speedups of 11.51 times (AFL++) to 14.66 times (AFLGo) over default seeds. On ARVO, SeedSmith enables fuzzers to trigger 16 previously unreachable bugs spanning 10 projects with diverse input formats.

</details>


### [161] [SLBench: Evaluating How LLM Agents Follow Logical Relations in Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09016)
*Xuan Chen,Chengpeng Wang,Lu Yan,Xiangyu Zhang*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出SkillLogic框架，用于分析技能文件中的逻辑关系并构建可执行测试。扫描5000+公开技能发现70%包含逻辑关系，构建SLBench基准测试（86个案例），评估显示LLM智能体不安全率高达70%，而SLGuard防护可将违规减少63%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体技能的安全性取决于解析交互指令间的依赖关系，现有工作缺乏对技能文件中逻辑关系的系统性分析与测试方法。

Method: 提出SkillLogic框架，定义八种逻辑关系类型（前提条件、约束、回退等）；扫描5000+公开技能；构建SLBench可执行基准；设计SLGuard推理时防护。

Result: 70%技能包含逻辑关系；Codex和Claude Code在六个LLM骨干上不安全率达70%，导致隐私泄露、不安全配置变更和清理不完整；SLGuard减少63%违规。

Conclusion: 逻辑关系遵循是技能引导智能体面临的一个独特的可靠性挑战，需要针对性解决。

Abstract: Agent skills extend LLM agents with reusable procedures, tools, and domain-specific workflows, but their safety depends on resolving dependencies among interacting instructions. We introduce SkillLogic, a framework for analyzing logical relations in skill files and constructing executable tests from them. Our taxonomy covers eight relation types, including preconditions that gate valid actions, constraints that limit how allowed actions may be performed, and fallbacks that specify recovery behavior after failure. Using SkillLogic, we scan over 5000 public skills and find that 70% contain at least one logical relation. We then construct SLBench, an 86-case executable benchmark from high-confidence, high-impact, and locally testable relations. Evaluating Codex and Claude Code across six LLM backbones shows unsafe rates up to 70%, with violations leading to privacy leaks, unsafe configuration changes, and incomplete cleanup. The human audit attributes failures to both agent capability gaps and low-salience skill text. We further show that SLGuard, a lightweight inference-time scaffold, reduces violations by 63% on targeted cases. Our results establish logical-relation following as a distinct reliability challenge for skill-guided agents.

### [162] [Malaika: Understanding Malware through Tri-Grounded Agentic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09179)
*Xingzhi Qian,Xinran Zheng,Yiling He,Lorenzo Cavallaro*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出Malaika框架，通过三重接地（领域接地、语义接地、知识接地）将恶意软件理解形式化为有根据的推理问题，实验表明该方法能产生更精确、可审计的分析结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 恶意软件分析面临核心挑战：分析者需要在部分可观测性下，从稀疏分散且与良性功能交织的证据中重建高层恶意行为。现有LLM系统在安全代码分析方面表现不错，但恶意软件理解的可靠性不足，关键在于缺乏对证据是否足以支撑行为级结论的严格判断。

Method: 提出三重接地机制：(1) 领域接地——约束行为假设的生成与评估；(2) 语义接地——定位并连接程序中的支持性证据；(3) 知识接地——通过外部可验证威胁知识进行行为归因。基于此设计Malaika多智能体框架，包含分析师启发的推理、工具中介的证据定位和基于检索的行为归因。在Android恶意软件分析上实例化并评估。

Result: Malaika在恶意软件理解任务上优于先前的LLM分析框架；与专业分析系统和前沿智能体框架的对比表明，接地感知推理能产生更精确、可审计的结论；消融实验支持了接地假设的有效性。

Conclusion: 接地感知推理为可靠的恶意软件理解提供了有原则的基础，并且更广泛地，也为基于证据的软件分析提供了方法论支撑。可靠性不仅取决于模型能力，还取决于推理过程本身。

Abstract: Recent LLM-based systems have shown promising capabilities for security-focused code analysis. Malware understanding, however, poses a distinct challenge: analysts must reconstruct high-level malicious behaviors under partial observability from sparse, dispersed evidence intertwined with benign functionality. While static analysis can expose security-relevant signals, the central challenge is not merely identifying suspicious code, but determining whether the evidence sufficiently supports an auditable behavior-level conclusion. We formulate malware understanding as a grounded reasoning problem and argue that reliable behavior reconstruction requires three complementary forms of grounding. Domain grounding constrains how behavior hypotheses are generated and evaluated, semantics grounding localizes and connects supporting program evidence, and knowledge grounding supports behavioral attribution through externally verifiable threat knowledge. To study this hypothesis, we present Malaika, a multi-agent framework that operationalizes the three grounding mechanisms through analyst-inspired reasoning, tool-mediated evidence localization, and retrieval-based behavioral attribution. We instantiate Malaika for Android malware analysis and evaluate it on malware-understanding tasks. Results show that Malaika improves analysis quality over prior LLM-based malware-analysis frameworks and demonstrate that reliability depends not only on model capability but also on the reasoning process. In particular, comparisons against malware-analysis systems and frontier agentic frameworks show that grounding-aware reasoning produces more precise and auditable conclusions. Ablation studies further support the grounding hypothesis. These findings suggest that grounding-aware reasoning provides a principled foundation for reliable malware understanding and, more broadly, for evidence-grounded software analysis.

</details>


### [163] [RaMark: Radioactive Watermarking for Generated Tabular Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09000)
*Xin Che,Lingyang Chu,Qiqi Zhang,Xinyu Ma,Xuan Luo,Jian Pei*

Main category: cs.CR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有水印方法在重训练攻击下失效——攻击者用水印数据集重训练生成模型后，生成的数据不再携带水印。需要一种能在模型重训练后仍保持水印可检测性的方法。

Method: 提出RaMark，通过将正弦依赖作为数据分布的内在组成部分嵌入，使水印与底层分布耦合。任何保留数据效用的生成模型必须同时保留水印，否则将降低效用或改变数据分布。

Result: 在两个真实表格数据集上，在包含10^5个独立数据所有者的所有权验证场景下，RaMark在放射性（重训练后水印可检测性）上显著优于7种SOTA方法，并在重训练和数据修改攻击中持续表现更好。

Conclusion: RaMark通过将水印与数据分布耦合实现了放射性特性，理论和实验均证明其能有效抵御重训练攻击，为隐私敏感的表格数据共享提供了更可靠的所有权验证方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in generative modeling have made generated tabular data a practical solution for privacy-sensitive data sharing, where watermarking enables ownership verification. However, existing watermarking methods fundamentally fail under retraining attacks, in which an adversary retrains a generative model on a watermarked dataset and regenerates high-utility data that no longer carries the watermark. We address this challenge by introducing radioactivity, the property that a watermark remains detectable after generative model retraining, and propose RaMark, a radioactive watermarking method that embeds a sinusoidal dependency as an intrinsic component of the data distribution. By coupling the watermark with the underlying distribution, RaMark ensures that any generative model preserving data utility also has to preserve the watermark. We theoretically show that with high probability removing watermark degrades utility and alters data distribution. Extensive experiments on two real-world tabular datasets, under a large-scale ownership verification setting with $10^5$ independent data owners, demonstrate that RaMark achieves substantially stronger radioactivity than seven state-of-the-art methods and consistently outperforms them against both retraining and data modification attacks.

</details>

To improve physical consistency, the second law of thermodynamics is incorporated as a training constraint by enforcing non-negative entropy generation, which restricts the evolution of the thermochemical state to physically admissible directions and improves stability during time integration. The approach is demonstrated on DNS of a two-dimensional planar lean premixed methane-air flame interacting with a turbulent flow field. The model reproduces detailed-chemistry results with high fidelity while achieving more than an order-of-magnitude reduction in computational cost. On top of SPAM, we introduce two simple but effective lightweight, gradient-descent-free prediction heads: a recognition head and a segmentation head. Our method requires less than a minute of phonetic transcriptions, and generalizes to unseen phones during training. Across a diverse range of datasets, our approach attains strong segmentation and recognition performance.

### [167] [Wireless Decentralized Federated Learning via Device Clustering and Inter-Cluster Link Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08797)
*William Weijia Zheng,Hang Liu,Ying-Jun Angela Zhang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 针对无线去中心化联邦学习（DFL）中因点对点模型交换导致收敛慢的问题，本文提出一种预算感知的聚类中心DFL框架：先对网络进行稠密聚类，再将有限回程链路分配给聚类头节点，形成簇内快速并行聚合与簇间稀疏交换的两层协议，实现了O(1/t)的收敛速度，在图像分类任务上显著加速了收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无线DFL中，点对点模型聚合存在高延迟和误差，特别是在大规模且具有聚类结构的D2D网络中，多对多梯度共享导致信道接入不协调、落后者通信误差大、模型共识缓慢，形成聚合瓶颈。

Method: 提出预算感知的聚类中心DFL框架：（1）将网络划分为密集连接的簇；（2）将有限的回程链路预算分配给选定的簇头节点；（3）构建两层协议：簇内快速并行聚合 + 簇间（头节点间）低频交换。

Result: 理论收敛率为O(1/t)；在图像分类任务上的数值实验表明，仅需少量策略性部署的回程链路即可显著加速收敛，优于现有DFL基线方法。

Conclusion: 通过在落后者节点上布设少量可靠回程链路增强网络连通性，结合聚类思想，可有效缓解无线DFL的聚合瓶颈，实现快速、高效的分布式学习。

Abstract: Decentralized federated learning (DFL) dispenses with the central server of classical FL by utilizing peer-to-peer model exchanges among edge devices. This server-free architecture enables ad-hoc, flexible distributed learning in large device-to-device (D2D) networks. However, wireless DFL converges slowly because peer-to-peer model aggregation incurs high delays and errors. Each DFL training round involves many-to-many gradient sharing over wireless channels, resulting in uncoordinated channel access, large communication errors from stragglers, and slow model consensus, especially in large-scale D2D networks with pronounced clustering structures. We address these aggregation bottlenecks by provisioning a few reliable backhaul links at straggling nodes to enhance network connectivity. Building on this idea, our budget-aware, cluster-centric DFL framework first partitions the network into densely connected clusters, and then allocates the limited backhaul budget to selected cluster heads. The resulting two-tier protocol executes fast, parallel model aggregation within clusters and infrequent inter-cluster exchanges among the heads, yielding an O(1/t) convergence rate in t iterations. Numerical experiments on image-classification tasks confirm that our approach accelerates convergence compared to state-of-the-art DFL baselines with only a few strategically placed backhaul links.

### [169] [Influence Diagnostics in High-dimensional M-estimation: Precise Asymptotics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09250)
*Hugo Cui*

Main category: stat.ML

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的低维大样本极限下，leave-one-out影响量的统计特性已很清晰，但在高维场景下（n ≍ d），样本影响会与其他训练样本产生复杂依赖关系，现有理论尚不完善，亟需高维理论刻画。

Method: 针对高斯设计下的凸M估计问题，在高维极限（n ≍ d）下，理论推导了训练集上影响量的分布收敛到某个极限测度，并给出该测度的精确刻画。

Result: 证明了高维场景下训练样本影响量的分布收敛到可精确刻画的极限测度；同时发现高影响样本倾向于靠近决策边界。

Conclusion: 该理论结果与主动学习中"选择靠近决策边界的样本"这一经典启发式方法建立了联系，为数据选择策略提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: The impact of a given training point on a statistical model is classically measured through its leave-one-out influence, which quantifies the effect of its removal from the training set on the model accuracy. While the statistics of leave-one-out influences are well understood in the low-dimensional, large sample limit $n\to \infty, d=O(1)$, they become more intricate in high dimensions, as the influence of a given sample develops non-trivial dependencies on all other training samples. For convex M-estimation under Gaussian design, in the high-dimensional limit $n\asymp d$, we show that the distribution of the influences across the training set converges to a limiting measure which we sharply characterize. Building on these results, we provide evidence that influential samples tend to lie close to the decision boundary, thereby making contact with a standard data selection heuristic in active learning.

</details>


### [170] [Spectrally Deconfounded Gradient Boosting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09371)
*Andrea Nava,Peter Bühlmann,Fabio Sigrist*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于梯度提升的非线性谱去混方法，通过谱损失与正则化（特别是早停）的交互作用来缓解隐藏混杂问题，并提供了混合模型解释和经验贝叶斯调参方法，实验表明该方法在目标函数估计上优于现有基线且更具扩展性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 灵活的机器学习方法容易受到隐藏混杂因素的影响——模型可能学到由未观测混杂变量引起的虚假关联，而非稳定的真实信号。现有谱去混方法主要局限于线性模型，缺乏对非线性场景的有效处理。

Method: 提出非线性谱去混框架用于梯度提升：将普通平方误差损失替换为谱损失，通过减缓混杂对齐方向的学习速度来改变提升动力学。核心发现是去混效果不仅来自谱损失本身，更来自谱收缩与正则化（尤其是早停）的交互作用。此外，提供混合模型解释连接LAVA型收缩与随机效应调整，并给出经验贝叶斯调参方法，通过拉普拉斯近似和核随机效应扩展到一般似然和非线性混杂。

Result: 在合成数据和真实世界实验中，谱去混梯度提升在隐藏混杂下改进了目标函数的估计，且比现有的非线性谱去混基线方法具有更好的可扩展性。

Conclusion: 谱损失与早停正则化的结合是去混的关键，混合模型视角为参数调优提供了理论依据，该方法在非线性场景下有效且可扩展。

Abstract: Flexible machine-learning methods can be sensitive to hidden confounding: they may learn associations induced by unobserved confounders rather than stable signals. Spectral deconfounding mitigates this problem by shrinking high-variance directions of the covariate matrix that, under dense confounding, carry latent confounder information. Existing work has largely focused on linear models. We develop a nonlinear spectral deconfounding framework for gradient boosting. Our approach replaces the ordinary squared-error loss by a spectral loss, which alters the boosting dynamics by slowing down learning in confounding-aligned directions. We show that deconfounding is not achieved by the spectral loss alone, but by the interaction between spectral shrinkage and regularization, especially in terms of early stopping. Moreover, we provide a mixed-model interpretation that connects LAVA-type shrinkage to random-effects adjustment and yields an empirical-Bayes procedure for tuning the spectral loss. We also extend the method to general likelihoods and nonlinear confounding using Laplace approximations and kernel random effects. Across synthetic and real-world experiments, spectrally deconfounded boosting improves estimation of the target function under hidden confounding and is substantially more scalable than existing nonlinear spectral deconfounding baselines.

</details>


### [171] [Deep Gaussian Processes on Directed Acyclic Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09645)
*Federico L. Perlino,Oliver Hamelijnck,Adam M. Johansen,Theodoros Damoulas*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于深度高斯过程（DGP）的有向无环图（DAG）建模框架，用于处理在DAG上部分观测、带噪声且异质采样的组合函数。作者从理论上研究了先验坍缩行为、图拓扑和信息保存的关系，提出了保持依赖关系的结构化变分近似方法，并在多个任务上取得了SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多现实过程（如因果机制、多保真度工程、基因调控网络）可表示为DAG上的函数组合，但面临部分观测、噪声干扰和异质采样等挑战，现有方法难以有效重建、传播不确定性和进行推断。

Method: 将深度高斯过程扩展到DAG结构上，为每个节点上的函数放置高斯过程先验；理论分析了先验坍缩行为与图拓扑的关系；提出了一种结构化变分近似方法，保留图依赖关系、组合不确定性并捕捉collider节点的解释消除行为。

Result: 理论方面：获得了输入区分度保持的渐近频率的几乎必然下界，识别了推广的核类，证明了输入连接的作用。实验方面：在潜在collider DAG、蛋白质信号网络和多保真度重离子碰撞仿真任务上达到SOTA，同时恢复了低保真度贡献并具有可解释性。

Conclusion: DGP-DAG框架有效解决了DAG上组合函数建模的挑战，理论分析和实验验证均表明其优越性，为因果推断、多保真度建模和基因调控网络分析提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Many real-world processes can be represented as compositions of functions along a directed acyclic graph (DAG). In causal modelling, these correspond to the underlying mechanisms; in engineering, to multiple fidelity levels; and in gene-regulatory networks, to transcription factors. These functions are partially observed across the DAG, with noisy and heterogeneously sampled measurements, posing significant challenges for reconstruction, uncertainty propagation, and inference. To tackle these challenges, we place priors over functions and naturally arrive at Deep Gaussian Processes over DAGs. We theoretically study their prior-collapse behaviour, and the effect of graph topology and intermediate observations on the preservation of information. We obtain almost-sure lower bounds on the asymptotic frequency of depths at which the distinction between inputs is preserved, identify broad kernel classes for which these hold, and prove an observation by \cite{dunlop2018} on the role of input connections. We offer a structured variational approximation that retains graph dependencies, preserves compositional uncertainty, and captures the explaining-away behaviour of colliders. Finally, we empirically validate our theoretical results and our methodology, and model a latent-collider DAG, a protein signalling network, and a multi-fidelity heavy-ion collision emulation task, attaining state-of-the-art performance while recovering low-fidelity contributions and yielding interpretability of the simulator hierarchy.

</details>

### [172] [LLM for EDA in Front-End Design: Challenges and Opportunities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09616)
*Kangwei Xu,Bing Li,Ulf Schlichtmann*

Main category: cs.ET

TL;DR: 本文综述了大语言模型（LLMs）在芯片前端设计中的进展，探讨了EDA从局部辅助向自主智能体执行演变的趋势，并总结了关键挑战与未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着芯片复杂度增加和上市时间压力增大，前端设计成为芯片开发的瓶颈。LLMs在EDA中展现出巨大潜力，有望作为统一智能接口，推动EDA从局部辅助向自主智能体执行演变。

Method: 本文首先讨论EDA的演变趋势，然后综述LLMs在前端设计中的代表性进展，重点关注从共享规范生成电路和测试平台、以及在高层次综合等流程中提升设计质量。最后讨论关键挑战与未来机遇。

Result: LLMs在HDL生成、测试平台构建、设计空间探索等任务中展现出潜力；OpenClaw等智能体系统为下一代EDA提供了战略路线图。

Conclusion: LLMs在EDA前端设计中潜力巨大，但仍面临关键挑战；未来应推进智能体AI技术，实现更自主、更高效的前端设计流程。

Abstract: As chip complexity increases and time-to-market pressures grow, front-end design has become a critical bottleneck in chip development. Recently, Large Language Models (LLMs) have shown great potential in Electronic Design Automation (EDA). Beyond specification understanding, LLMs show the potential to serve as a unified intelligent interface for hardware description language (HDL) generation, testbench construction, and design space exploration. The rise of agentic AI, represented by pioneering systems such as OpenClaw, offers a strategic roadmap for the next generation EDA. From this perspective, this paper discusses the evolution of EDA from localized assistance to autonomous agentic execution. Then, we review representative advances of LLMs in front-end design, focusing on key tasks such as circuit and testbench generation from a shared specification, as well as design quality improvement in established workflows such as high-level synthesis. Finally, we discuss the key challenges and limitations of integrating LLMs into EDA, and outline future opportunities for advancing LLM-enabled front-end design, offering a systematic perspective for researchers interested in leveraging agentic AI technologies for EDA.

</details>

### [173] [PHINN-EEG: Topological Time-Series Analysis of Dream-State EEG -- Dynamic Betti Curves for Dream Content Classification and Topology-Conditioned Neural Signal Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09662)
*Ren Takahashi,Emre Yusuf,Jayabrata Bhaduri*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文提出PHINN-EEG，首个将持久同调拓扑方法应用于EEG梦境检测的框架。通过滑动窗Takens嵌入和Vietoris-Rips过滤提取动态Betti曲线，结合拓扑条件流匹配，在DREAM数据库上目标AUC达0.82-0.90，超越传统PSD方法的0.70。还提出拓扑条件整流流模型用于梦境EEG合成及Betti转变原型假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EEG梦境检测依赖功率谱密度和统计矩特征，最高AUC仅约0.70，性能瓶颈明显。作者认为神经活动的相空间几何结构（而非单纯的频谱能量）可能包含更丰富的梦境状态信息，因此引入拓扑时间序列分析方法来捕捉神经活动的拓扑不变性。

Method: 1) 对多通道觉醒前EEG片段使用滑动窗Takens延迟嵌入重构相空间；2) 进行Vietoris-Rips过滤构建单纯复形；3) 提取动态Betti曲线作为拓扑特征；4) 结合拓扑条件流匹配（topology-conditioned flow matching）进行梦境检测；5) 提出拓扑条件整流流模型用于梦境EEG合成；6) 提出Betti转变原型作为连接拓扑与梦境报告分类的假设框架。

Result: 目标AUC达到0.82-0.90，显著优于现有PSD和catch22基准（AUC约0.70）。数据集为DREAM数据库的1,462次唤醒子集（来自263名参与者、3,191次唤醒的完整注册库）。

Conclusion: 如果验证成功，这标志着从频谱能量分析到相空间几何的范式转变，特别适用于神经科学中的罕见事件检测，对未来可穿戴BCI梦境监测具有潜在应用价值。不过Betti转变原型的分类学仍待实证验证。

Abstract: Current electroencephalography (EEG)-based dream detection relies on power spectral density (PSD) and statistical moment features, achieving a state-of-the-art area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (AUC) of approximately 0.70 on the DREAM database (Wong et al., 2025, Nature Communications). We introduce PHINN-EEG (Persistent Homology Inspired Neural Network for EEG), the first topological time-series framework for dream mentation analysis. Using sliding-window Takens delay embeddings and Vietoris-Rips filtrations on multichannel pre-awakening EEG epochs, we extract Dynamic Betti Curves that characterize the geometric architecture of neural activity, not merely its energy. These topological invariants, combined with topology-conditioned flow matching, are analytically projected to outperform existing PSD and catch22 benchmarks, targeting AUC = 0.82-0.90 on the 1,462-awakening open-access subset of the DREAM database (drawn from a full registry of 3,191 total awakenings from 263 participants across 20 independent laboratories). We further introduce a topology-conditioned rectified flow model for dream-state EEG synthesis-with a spectral-conditioned flow model of comparable feature dimensionality as an additional ablation baseline to isolate the value of topological conditioning specifically-and propose a set of candidate Betti transition archetypes linking topology to phenomenological dream report categories, presented as an exploratory hypothesis space pending empirical validation. If validated, this work represents a paradigm shift from spectral energy to phase-space geometry in neural rare-event detection, with potential future implications for wearable BCI dream monitoring.

</details>
